Internal Reorganization of the Police Organization 23

(Nanjing) The current organization of police agencies in our country is based on the organizational outline of public security bureaus at all levels promulgated by the Ministry of Interior in October of the 17th year of the Republic of China. It has been seven or eight years since this system was implemented, and it is felt that it is not yet sound, and the name of the public security bureau is also not entirely appropriate. At this time of serious national crisis, the stability of the region lies in the police. If such an important organization is not reorganized, it will not be able to fulfill its responsibilities. In view of this, the Ministry of Interior formulated an organizational outline for police agencies at all levels in July of this year, which was submitted for approval and promulgation. In addition, based on Article 16 of the outline, three provisional regulations on the organization of police agencies in provincial capitals, cities, and counties were separately drafted. Now, these three regulations have been promulgated nationwide by the Ministry of Interior on the 26th and will be implemented uniformly. Starting from New Year's Day of the 26th year of the Republic of China, they will all be changed to police bureaus. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 27th)

Berlin Correspondence

Germany and Japan Conclude Anti-Comintern Pact 37

— Lieshan

About a year ago, newspapers in various countries were already widely reporting that Germany and Japan were about to conclude a military alliance against Russia. Since then, this event has been frequently mentioned in private conversations. In recent weeks, German newspapers have published an unusually large amount of news about Japan. Simply reading the editorials in various newspapers, all expressing deep sympathy for Japan, many people felt that the degree of cooperation between the two countries had reached a mature stage. Especially in the last week or two, dispatches from Tokyo and Shanghai have increasingly indicated that the time for the announcement of the pact is approaching. In the past week, the German ambassador to Britain, Mr. Ribbentrop, Hitler's special envoy, has traveled back and forth between London and Berlin twice. Mr. Ribbentrop is a key figure in charge of the Nazi Party's foreign policy, and his actual power far exceeds that of the German Foreign Minister. His frequent travels naturally carry a significant mission. Indeed, the long-rumored German-Japanese pact was finally formally signed in Berlin on November 25th. It is also noteworthy that Mr. Ribbentrop represented Germany at the signing of the pact, rather than Foreign Minister Neurath.

At seven o'clock that evening, Dr. Goebbels, the German Minister of Propaganda, announced the news to the German people in a clear voice via wireless telephone. Goebbels' elation is something everyone can imagine. Because after the recent German-Italian alliance, there is now a German-Japanese alliance, and the isolated diplomatic situation of Germany over the years has been broken by half. Moreover, according to Dr. Goebbels, this pact is a valuable contribution to world peace, because with two such strong countries as Germany and Japan cooperating, the Communist International will have no way to use its tricks. The next day, all German newspapers welcomed the new pact in unison. Many newspapers were able to write editorials in accordance with Dr. Goebbels' intentions. Everyone agreed that Japan, like Germany, is being threatened by the Communist Party. The German-Japanese alliance is purely for saving human culture. Japan, it is said, is also an ancient cultural country!

Looking at the official text of the German-Japanese pact, the most important point is that from now on, the two countries will cooperate effectively and take effective measures to resist the International Communist Party, that is to say, domestic or foreign, direct or indirect communist actions. Whether these methods include military action is not specified in the pact. But what we should pay most attention to is Article 2 of the original text of the pact. According to the provisions of this article, Germany and Japan have the "right" to help a third country eliminate the Communist Party within its borders. In other words, Germany has the "right" to openly help General Franco oppose the Spanish Popular Front government, as long as General Franco publicly requests Germany's help. The reason is that the Madrid government is "a Communist Party." Under this premise, even Japan can, without our consent, automatically "suppress the Communists" for us, can't it? Since the Northeast Incident, hasn't Japan been "suppressing the Communists" for us every day? After this pact, is Germany also coming to join in? Indeed, there are more and more people with a sense of justice in the international community recently.

Why does Germany need to conclude this pact? Perhaps because it feels diplomatically isolated, it needs an allied country. But the most important purpose is naturally to contain Russia by allying with Japan, and to break the military agreement between France, Russia, and Czechoslovakia. In the event of a future war in Europe, at least Soviet Russia will have worries in the East. Why does Japan need this pact? Perhaps it hopes to obtain a European ally to contain the actions of Britain and Russia in the Far East, so that it can calmly invade China. According to many foreign newspapers, in addition to the express pact, there is also a secret pact attached. Since it is said to be secret, we naturally have no way of knowing. However, one thing that can be believed is that Germany will help Japan expand its air force. According to a US journalist who visited Japan a year ago, Japan's air force almost entirely uses German materials and German technical personnel. Now that it is said that the two countries are allied, then military cooperation cannot be avoided. On this point, we Chinese should not easily let it go.

Since Germany and Italy have cooperated closely, the atmosphere of organizing a "new crusade" in Europe to conquer Russia has suddenly become strong. Whether Germany really has a plan to expedition to Soviet Russia is something we cannot guess. On the other hand, it has nothing to do with us Chinese anyway, because the participants in the war are Germans and Russians, at most it is just a struggle between the international Fascist Party and the international Communist Party. However, according to some people, the conflict between Germany and Russia is still just a facade. First, Germany and Russia do not have a common border. Second, the more violently Germany and Russia attack each other recently, the more trade between the two countries increases at the same time. If there is really a war, why give weapons to the enemy? Therefore, the conclusion is that anti-Russian and anti-communist are smokescreens. In fact, Germany will probably have problems with Czechoslovakia and Poland in the future, and this military action is still nominally "anti-communist." Soviet Russia is just a supporting role, not the main target.

We don't know where Germany's ultimate goal lies. But we are very clear about Japan's future plans. What we feel very regrettable is that German newspapers only mentioned to Britain that the German-Japanese pact does not hinder Britain's Far East interests, while forgetting the interests of China, the true master of the Far East. In recent years, commercial relations between China and Germany have become increasingly developed, and many people are hoping to increase the friendship between the two countries through this. But at this time, such an unfortunate event has occurred. The German Nazi Party authorities may not know what kind of adverse effects the signing of the German-Japanese pact will have on China. The Chinese people and the Chinese government will encounter an unprecedented historical difficulty under this pact. Although this pact is nominally aimed at dealing with Soviet Russia and opposing the Communist Party, in reality, the Japanese think differently from the Germans. They are using this pact to deal with China.

Most Germans welcome this pact, the reason being that Japan has also come to participate in opposing Soviet Russia and opposing the Communist Party. In reality, Germany is probably going to be fooled by others again, just like in the last World War. How does Japan oppose the Communist Party and Soviet Russia? By building bunkers on the Great Wall of China, while at the same time promoting in German newspapers that this is the work of "preventing communism." How far is the Great Wall of China from the Soviet border? Who are these bunkers in this place aimed at? Such an illogical propaganda method, yet most German readers believe that it is a fact. This is naturally a matter of common sense.

When the German-Japanese pact was signed, the Japanese ambassador to France explained to the French Foreign Ministry that this pact was not aimed at dealing with Soviet Russia. Japan's only goal is to prevent communist activities in its own country and "neighboring areas." The next day, German newspapers published a dispatch from the Japanese Domei News Agency stating that Japan has decided to take strict measures to deal with the Communist Party, especially in the Three Eastern Provinces and North China. "Suppressing the Communists" in the Three Eastern Provinces and North China is Japan's original intention, and it is also a good topic for invading China.

The Japanese explanation of the German-Japanese pact is naturally much more straightforward than the German explanation! (November 26)

Page 5

Current Commentary

World Peace and Germany 38

— Xing

The situation in Europe seems to have reached a very serious stage. According to a Berlin dispatch, the German authorities announced a ban on young men freely leaving the country and ordered skilled workers to prepare for military service. Apparently, due to the deepening domestic economic crisis, Germany intends to launch an international war to divert people's attention. However, we do not need to be too pessimistic about world peace. On the one hand, if Germany wants to launch a war, it must have financial support internationally in order to sustain the war on the battlefield. However, as everyone knows, Germany's finances have long been exhausted due to the rearmament of the past four years. There is naturally not much hope of obtaining assistance from the international financial community to consolidate wartime finances. At present, the largest part of the world's wartime resources and finance is in the hands of the three major democratic countries of Britain, the United States, and France. These three countries have never openly provided assistance to Germany's military and financial affairs. If war breaks out, Germany will inevitably be in a state of financial blockade. In that case, even if Germany launches a war, it will not have a victorious future. Secondly, the power of world peace has obviously increased a lot in recent months. Since the establishment of the currency agreement between Britain, the United States, and France, the economic status of aggressive countries has become more isolated under the joint action of the three major democratic countries. Moreover, the cooperative relationship between Japan, Germany, and Italy has gradually become dispersed. First, Italy cannot cooperate with Germany in the control of the balance of power in the Mediterranean. After Prime Minister Mussolini issued a declaration, the air of the revival of the Stresa Front spread again. This is a major blow to German diplomacy. Second, Japan has recently formally expressed its willingness to negotiate with the United States on the provisions of Article 19 of the Washington Treaty. Such an expression in Japanese diplomacy cannot but be regarded as the germination of a new trend. If this view is correct, then although Germany is actively preparing for war now, its economic status and diplomatic relations can still delay the war crisis.

Stalin Reported Seriously Ill Again 39

Moscow: Foreign reports indicate Stalin is seriously ill. Although he was recently seen attending a special meeting of the Soviet, rumors of his serious illness have not been dispelled. Those who have seen him feel that he is weak and ailing greatly. It is claimed Stalin's illness stems from heart weakness and overexertion. It is widely believed that Molotov will be his successor. (Translated from Foreign Commentary by Zi Lin News)

Pope's Foot Ailment Worsens 40

Vatican City: The Pope suffered greatly last night due to constant, severe pain in his left leg. The Pope has been suffering from a foot ailment for several days, but unexpectedly, the ailment worsened suddenly last night while reciting the rosary. However, his overall health is said to be satisfactory. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Strong Earthquake in Japan's Kanto Region Yesterday Morning; Izu's Niijima Island Reportedly Completely Destroyed; Epicenter in Deep Seabed Nearby 41

(Tokyo) At approximately 9:15 AM on the 27th, a relatively strong earthquake was felt throughout most of the Kanto region and the southern part of the Chubu region, with the most intense tremors felt in Shizuoka Prefecture, Kanagawa Prefecture, and Chiba Prefecture. In some cases, even clocks stopped. The epicenter was located south of Nojimazaki in Chiba Prefecture, near the seabed off the coast of Oshima Island. The range of the earthquake appears to be quite wide. (Domei dispatch, 27th)

(Tokyo) The Central Meteorological Observatory issued the following statement regarding the earthquake that occurred on Niijima Island: At 9:15 AM on the 27th, part of the seabed 4,000 meters deep near Niijima Island in the Izu Islands, 10 kilometers below the surface, collapsed and caused an earthquake due to a fault. Niijima Island, which is near the epicenter, experienced a strong earthquake. Although aftershocks continue, there should be no danger. (Domei dispatch, 17th)

(Tokyo) According to a report from the Niijima Island police in the Izu Islands to the Metropolitan Police Department, an earthquake occurred on Niijima Island at 9:10 AM. Landslides and fissures have occurred within the jurisdiction, and many houses have collapsed. Investigations are currently underway. (Domei dispatch, 27th)

Izu Niijima Island: On the afternoon of the 26th, Niijima Island seemed to feel continuous earthquakes due to underground movements on the seabed. The islanders were deeply suspicious and fearful. At 9:15 AM on the 27th, a major strong earthquake occurred. Most of the stone buildings collapsed or developed cracks. Although wooden houses avoided collapse, they were severely tilted. All the mountains also had landslides, and the roads cracked, making walking dangerous. Fortunately, there seem to be no deaths or injuries at present. Only two or three people are missing in the mountains, so the youth groups are conducting searches. Because of the frequent earthquakes, the islanders are all trembling and temporarily have to sleep in the open. The entire island has prepared for fire prevention and prohibited lighting fires. Therefore, Niijima Island can be said to be a fireless island. In addition to the rain, there is no preparation, so the islanders who are outdoors are very sad. Also, Oshima Island and Miyake Island are safe and sound. (Domei dispatch, 27th)

(Tokyo) According to a report from the Niijima Honmura Village Office to the Tokyo Prefectural Office at 1:00 PM on the 27th, a major earthquake occurred on Niijima Island, and the houses were completely destroyed. The shocks continued, making it impossible to investigate. According to the news received by the Electrical Department of the Tokyo Telegraph and Telephone Bureau, all the power lines on the island were destroyed, making it difficult to restore them temporarily. (Domei dispatch, 27th)

Yokosuka: The Yokosuka Naval Base, upon receiving news that Niijima Island was completely destroyed, urgently dispatched a flying boat commanded by Lieutenant Fukuoka of the Naval Air Corps at 1:40 PM on the 27th to investigate the facts. (Domei dispatch, 27th)

Izu Niijima Island: An Island with Southern Flair, Natural Hot Springs and Scenic Views; Islanders Mostly Live by Fishing

(Tokyo) Izu Niijima Island, which is reported to have been completely destroyed, is located far at 24 degrees north latitude, surrounded by black seas, like a stone remotely tied within the Pacific Ocean, and is one of the Izu Seven Islands. It has 740 households and a population of over 4,000. The islanders engage in fishing and cultivate and manufacture camellia oil. The old and the young are all honest and simple, living and working in peace and contentment, with a strong southern atmosphere. The coastline is all white sand, and hot springs flow constantly through the rock crevices, harmonized by the tide. The islanders who have been blessed with this nature have recently operated the Niijima Hot Spring Hotel and five or six other inns, making it the most suitable health resort in the Kanto region. (Domei dispatch, 7th)

Canada's Participation in the Pan-American Group: Proponents and Opponents Each Have Reasons; Kellogg Praises Roosevelt Highly; Hull Leads Delegation Away From Buenos Aires to Return Home 44

(Washington) After the close of the Pan-American Peace Conference, international circles here have been widely discussing the possibility of Canada's future participation in the Pan-American peace coordination. Well-informed sources have learned that the reasons for both proponents and opponents are as follows: A. Reasons for proponents: (1) After Canada's participation, the American peace group can extend from the South Pole to the North Pole. In the event that Canada faces the danger of aggression in the future, it can obtain new diplomatic assistance. (2) Canada also has considerable commercial and financial relations with Latin American countries, so it can obtain most-favored-nation treatment. (3) If the United States participates in the system of controlling armaments or restricting trade with belligerent countries, the risk of American factories relocating to Canada can be avoided. (4) Pan-American cooperation is almost entirely in the technical and cultural fields, and Canada's participation can facilitate all aspects. B. Reasons for opponents: (1) Canada's relationship with the British Empire will make the close relationship between the dominion and the independent countries of America illogical, and may cause inconvenience to London. (2) After cooperating with South American countries, Canada cannot simultaneously maintain commercial ties with various parts of the Empire, because the agricultural products of South American countries are in competition with Canada's products. (3) If British Canada can participate in the Pan-American Group, then the territories of the Netherlands and France, such as the West Indies, can of course also participate. In this way, the Pan-American movement will have a Europeanized color. (4) In the event of unexpected events, Canada's activities in the Pan-American Group will be difficult to handle because it must consider London's opinions. (National News dispatch, 26th)

Mr. Kellogg, the former Secretary of State of Minnesota, USA, who jointly initiated the Paris Peace Pact with French Foreign Minister Briand, gave a speech here, praising President Roosevelt, saying that he has been diligently seeking sincerity and trust among nations, and said, "The President's personal visit to Central and South America to complete the mission of peace is enough to make other countries follow suit and work together for peace. I am very pleased with this. If countries are currently at war, the leader of the war will be the first to suffer. This is something that the most important countries in the world today must recognize." Finally, Kellogg said that he firmly believes that the United States will do its best to continue working to maintain international peace. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Buenos Aires, Argentina: The Pan-American Peace Conference, which opened on the 1st of this month, has now concluded. The US delegation, led by Secretary of State Hull, set off today to return home. Argentine government officials and representatives from various countries attending the conference went to the port to see them off. Most of the people also cheered and paid tribute to Hull. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Philippine Independence Issue 46

(Washington) Senator King, who supports the early simultaneous guarantee of Philippine independence by all countries of the world, told the Associated Press today that the independence and economic development of the Philippines should not be endangered in the slightest, and that guaranteeing the development of autonomous government is best achieved through an international neutrality agreement. The Philippines can also be a dangerous place in the Far East, so he opposes the establishment of a naval base in the Philippines. For 20 years, he has never believed that Japan coveted the Philippines, but today it is very different from the past. He only hopes that Japan can also participate in the above-mentioned neutrality agreement. As for the point that the Philippines is protected by the United States, King also opposes it. He believes that after the Philippines is completely independent, even if it is attacked by other countries, the United States should not fight for it, but only accept the fait accompli like Abyssinia. (Berlin) The case of the German ship "Palos" being intercepted by a Spanish government warship yesterday is indeed feared to cause a serious international dispute. The German authorities held an emergency meeting in Berchtesgaden and immediately ordered several warships to sail at full speed to Bilbao. It is generally believed that there are currently about six to nine German warships in Spanish territorial waters. These ships have recently been anchored in Gibraltar, Málaga, and San Sebastian. When we arrived in Limoges, France, the local police tried to stop us, but we were unmoved. It can be seen that we are indeed determined." We are new recruits from the 1933 and 1935 classes. Agreement on Maintaining the Status Quo in the Mediterranean; British-Italian Agreement Drafted; Signing to Take Place Soon; Full Text to Be Published Today or Tomorrow 60

(Rome) The gentlemen's agreement between Britain and Italy on the Mediterranean issue was drafted three days ago and sent to London to solicit the opinions of the British government. Once the British side provides a response, the signing can take place. The draft agreement is divided into four or five sections, the most difficult of which is the section on both sides respecting the existing status in the Mediterranean. Initially, both sides intended to mutually promise to maintain the naval balance of power in the Mediterranean, but because the composition of the British and Italian Mediterranean fleets is very different (the British battleships are more numerous than the Italian fleet), it was necessary to abandon this proposal and replace it with the phrase "respect the existing status" to make it more flexible. Not only should the naval tonnage of both sides maintain the status quo (the British naval tonnage in the Mediterranean is 100,000 to 125,000 tons more than that of Italy), but the naval bases established by both sides should also maintain the status quo. The ongoing projects (Britain is building naval bases in Haifa Port in Palestine, and Italy is building naval bases in the Dodecanese Islands in the eastern Mediterranean) can still be continued by both sides. The above sections are not detailed in the agreement, but are only a matter of gentleman's faith, but they are extremely important in spirit. The dispute between Britain and Italy has been delayed for more than a year and can now be brought to an end, and the general atmosphere can be eased. Furthermore, the gentleman's agreement is not aimed at any other country, and the signatories mutually agree to work for the cause of peace. The route from Britain to India and the route from Italy to East Africa are guaranteed by both sides. (Havas News Agency Telegram, 26th)

(Rome) It is reported that British Ambassador to Italy Drummond visited Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano at 11:00 this morning to discuss matters. Therefore, the gentleman's agreement between Britain and Italy on the Mediterranean issue can be established quickly. The full text will likely be published next Monday or Tuesday. It is reported that its content is very brief, not exceeding twenty lines typed on a typewriter. It only states that Britain and Italy mutually guarantee to maintain peace and freedom of navigation in the Mediterranean and mutually respect the existing status in the Mediterranean. The last level is the most difficult point of negotiation. According to reports, Italian officer Count Rossi led Italian troops to Mallorca Island in the Spanish Balearic Islands in the Mediterranean in September to set up defenses, with the intention of staying on the island for a long time. This matter was a major reef in the relationship between Britain and Italy in the Mediterranean. However, it is now reported that Count Rossi withdrew from the island ten days ago, and the negotiation of the gentleman's agreement between the two countries was able to take a sudden turn for the better, apparently facilitated by this move. Furthermore, general observers believe that there will be no provisions on various naval technical issues in the agreement. However, Italy's future attitude towards the Spanish events will be changed by this agreement. If so, the general situation in Europe can be eased. The most important issue thereafter is the German issue. Opinion here expresses support for the rapprochement between France and Germany and between Britain and Germany, believing that the foundation for this rapprochement should lie in (1) Germany abolishing its policy of economic self-sufficiency and restoring normal economic relations with other countries, and (2) that country revising its arms policy. (Havas Telegram, 26th)

All Circles in Beiping Celebrate Commander-in-Chief Chiang's Escape; Students from More Than 30 Schools Hold Parades; Song Zheyuan Speaks to Express Happiness 67

Beiping Correspondence: After the news of Commander-in-Chief Chiang's escape and arrival in Luoyang at 6:00 PM on the 25th reached Beiping, all newspapers immediately published special editions. Newspaper boys also shouted wildly on the streets, spreading the news throughout the city. After 7:00 PM, students from various schools set off firecrackers to celebrate. Starting at 8:00 AM, they set off in groups, carrying slogans celebrating and supporting Commander-in-Chief Chiang and posting them throughout the city. It is estimated that more than 30 middle schools and universities participated in the parade, with nearly 20,000 male and female students wearing military training uniforms or uniforms, showing great enthusiasm. When the students were parading in the morning, the Beiping police, who had been ordered to be on alert in recent days to prevent student unrest, thought that the student parade on the 26th was such a preparation, so they tried to stop it. Yang Likui, a professor at Normal University, and others went to the city government to visit Mayor Qin Decun to explain their intentions, saying that the student parade was celebratory in nature and that the students from various schools were being supervised by teachers and would not have any accidents. Qin sent personnel to inform the police to let them go and ordered Chen Jiyan, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to send mounted police to protect them. After Yang and others left, the police also received orders, and the students continued the parade. At noon, a general meeting was held in front of Tiananmen Square until 1:30 PM, and the meeting was adjourned. In the afternoon, the parade continued until about 5:00 PM, when they lined up and returned to school.

After Song Zheyuan heard that Commander-in-Chief Chiang had escaped, he made a statement on the morning of the 26th, saying, "I received telegrams last night proving that Commander-in-Chief Chiang has escaped. In addition to sending a telegram to Luoyang that night to express my condolences to Commander-in-Chief Chiang, I also see this as a blessing for the country and the people. After the Xi'an Incident occurred, I received a telegram from Zhang Hanqing and immediately replied, expressing two points: (1) I have always supported the central government, and (2) I resolutely implement the anti-communist policy. Later, I heard that the government thoroughly rectified the disciplinary net, and I believed that the border officials should obey the central government's主張when the leader suffered such an accident so that they could quell the situation as soon as possible. I also hope that Zhang Hanqing can accommodate the opinions of all parties as soon as possible to maintain the prestige of the central government and the dignity of the leader. I am very pleased that the incident has been peacefully resolved. From now on, my policy is to support the government and thoroughly eliminate the communists." (26th)

Under a Certain Party's Poisoning Policy: An Overview of Tianjin's Anti-Drug Efforts - 2,000 Drug Cases, Eleven Executions 68

Over Four Hundred Opium Dens Operate Openly Under the Protection of Concessions

Tianjin Dispatch: Since the central government stipulated a two-year ban on drugs and a six-year ban on opium, Tianjin, despite its special environment, has strived to implement these policies, dealing a blow to a certain party's poisoning policy. As the end of the year approaches, the term for the drug ban is coming to a close. Drug offenders have only about ten days left to live. From January 1st of next year, anyone caught will be executed immediately. Here is a summary of Tianjin's anti-drug achievements and progress over the past two years:

Drugs Within Concessions

The types of drugs, according to the Strict Prohibition of Highly Addictive Drugs Ordinance, are divided into several types, including opium, gold pills, red pills, morphine, and white pills. Among them, opium is the most prevalent. Its source is opium dens within a certain concession. Within a certain concession, besides Rue de Chusan, opium dens are found everywhere in the streets and alleys. Most are run by Koreans and operate openly under the protection of a certain party. The total number reaches more than four hundred and twenty. Drug addicts flock there day and night. Each opium den is crowded with people, the business is thriving, forming a grand spectacle. The municipal authorities have repeatedly sent notes to a certain concession, requesting them to investigate and prohibit these activities, but to no avail. The implementation of a certain party's poisoning policy cannot be effectively stopped. Recently, many Koreans have been carrying bags filled with drugs, peddling them in the counties and villages of the interior. The Hebei Provincial Government, upon receiving reports, specially dispatched Councilor Chen Shusheng to various counties to, together with local authorities, monitor Koreans leaving the country and hand them over to the Tianjin Japanese Police Department for handling. As of this month, eleven batches, totaling eighty-three people, have been apprehended.

Establishment of Rehabilitation Centers

At the beginning of the drug ban implementation, the first thing was to establish rehabilitation facilities to help addicts quit. In the spring of the previous year, when Zhang Ting'e was the mayor of Tianjin, despite the city treasury being severely strained, he managed to prepare and establish a rehabilitation center with five hundred beds, accommodating addicts who voluntarily sought treatment or were caught in drug cases. At that time, those who had a slight desire to reform flocked to seek rehabilitation, including university students, former county magistrates, secretaries, or government officials. Currently, for the sake of easier management, the municipal government has merged the rehabilitation center into the Municipal Second Hospital, but the scale and organization remain the same. According to the statistics released by the center, from the date of its establishment to the end of November of this year, a total of 14,621 people have been rehabilitated, with women accounting for six percent. However, according to estimates, the total number of drug addicts in the city reaches 60,000, so only one-sixth of them have been rehabilitated in the past two years. The center is now preparing to close down. From January 1st of next year, drug offenders will be executed. It is unknown where these 50,000 drug addicts will be placed.

Statistics on Drug Cases

The Municipal Government, in order to handle cases involving highly addictive drugs, specially established the Drug Case Trial Office. It began operating on January 1, 1935. Most of the cases accepted were those captured by the Tianjin Public Security Bureau. Occasionally, a few were transferred from the Tianjin Security Command for trial. The total number of drug cases is about two thousand, involving more than three thousand criminals. Among them, eleven have been executed by firing squad, including two for manufacturing drugs, three for trafficking drugs, three for transporting drugs, and three for relapse. The remaining were sentenced to imprisonment ranging from twenty days to fifteen years. After all judgments were made, they were submitted to the Hebei-Chahar-Suiyuan Pacification Commissioner's Office for approval and then transferred to the Hebei Third Prison for execution. Currently, the office still has more than eighty pending cases, which are being cleared. It is also scheduled to close at the end of this year. Because the date for executing drug offenders is approaching, the municipal government has specially ordered all agencies to conduct anti-drug publicity, with cautionary slogans and startling murals visible everywhere. The Public Education Center is also holding parades and performing the drama "Shooting Opium Addicts" to promote the awakening of drug addicts.

Municipal Government Burns Drugs

In order to demonstrate its determination to ban drugs, the Tianjin Municipal Government specifically scheduled a drug burning at 2:00 PM on the 28th of this month next to the rehabilitation center outside the main station. From the June 3rd Opium Prohibition Day commemoration to November 30th, a total of 8,585 taels, 6 mace, 1 candareen, and 5 ho of raw opium and opium paste, and 2,546 taels, 5 mace, 0 candareen, 7 li, 4 hao, and 5 si of drugs were seized and newly collected. All were burned publicly. In addition to preparing a list and submitting it to the Hebei-Chahar-Suiyuan Pacification Commissioner's Office for approval, notices have also been sent to various agencies and organizations, inviting them to send personnel to supervise the event to ensure solemnity. According to Ma Yanchong, the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, from January 1st of next year, anyone who manufactures, traffics, or uses drugs will be executed immediately upon capture, regardless of any difficulties. For this purpose, Peiping has purchased two thousand coffins for standby. This city can do the same if necessary. (23rd)

Southern Fujian: Poisoned Salt Incident in Yongchun - Official Salt Transport to Yongchun Blocked, Public Food Supply Feared - Quanzhou Salt Bureau Denies Poisoning 69

Xiamen Dispatch: A recent incident of poisoned salt in Yongchun County, Southern Fujian, has caused public panic. Previously, on the 21st, the Shuide Salt Bureau transported a batch of new salt from Quanzhou. On the same day, the Taixing Store in Wulijie, Yongchun, began selling the new salt that night. After eating the salt, soldiers of the First Company of the 11th Security Regiment stationed in the county experienced collective abdominal pain. Inspection of the food and cooking utensils revealed nothing unusual. It was decided to test the newly purchased salt, and it was discovered to contain nitric acid and mercury, poisonous substances. The regimental headquarters, based on the situation, immediately sent troops to investigate together with the district office. However, the person in charge of Taixing Store had already fled. On the 22nd, the regimental headquarters sealed up the salt stored in Taixing Store and the Yongde Official Salt Distribution Center, and sent troops to guard it. Within a few hours, the news spread throughout the city. Those who had purchased the new salt dared not eat it, and those without salt dared not buy more. It was found that the Salt Bureau had transported a total of 3,000 dan of new salt this time. On the afternoon of the 22nd, twelve salt boats from the Second District were transported upstream from Jinjiang and were also monitored by troops sent by the regimental headquarters, who were not allowed to unload and sell the cargo. Zhang Kewu, the commander of the 11th Security Regiment, telegraphed the Quanzhou Salt Bureau, stating that the poisonous salt had been sealed and that it was hoped that good salt would be transported to Yongchun as soon as possible to alleviate the salt shortage. As a result, the price of old salt originally stored in Yongchun rose sharply, selling for one dime per catty, yet people remained suspicious and hesitant, resulting in panic. However, the Quanzhou Salt Affairs Bureau denied the poisoning. On the 23rd, a notice was issued in Yongchun, stating: "Case investigation shows that on December 22nd of this year, Wang Bin, the distributor of the Yongde Official Salt Distribution Center, reported that the district office, together with the military, surrounded the Penglai Official Salt Retail Store, claiming that the salt sold contained poisonous substances. Investigation reveals that the salt was indeed transported from the Quanzhou General Office and there are no anomalies. Please telegraph the Yongchun 11th Regiment headquarters and the county government to stop the situation. Based on this, investigation reveals that all official salt distributed by various retail stores belonging to the Yongde Distribution Center was transported from this office. The official salt of this office is entirely from formal salt fields and has undergone chemical testing before leaving the factory. Since no accidents have occurred elsewhere, it is incomprehensible why there is a rumor of poisonous substances in a corner of the Wulizhen area. In addition to telegraphing military and government agencies to send personnel to conduct on-site investigations, this notice is hereby issued to the people of Shuide and counties for their information (omitted below)." However, the salt has not been unsealed as of the 24th, and people dare not buy salt. The Salt Bureau is currently conducting a thorough investigation together with the county government and the regimental headquarters. (December 27th)

Songjiang: Water Patrol Captures Bandits 70

Since the implementation of winter defense in this county, robberies have occurred frequently in Punan. Magistrate Li immediately ordered the water patrol team to set out and patrol. On the 21st, Captain Fei led the team to Hougang in the Seventh District. That evening, the home of Lu Youcai in that area was robbed. The team sent investigators to investigate. Soon, informants reported that Cao Ahe seemed to be a bad character. The team happened to be in a restaurant in Zhangze and apprehended Cao. Two pawn tickets from the 22nd and a pearl hairpin were found on his person. He denied the charges during interrogation. Later, investigators took the stolen goods to the homes of the robbery victims for investigation and confirmed that they were indeed the stolen items. The suspect then confessed without denying anything. He also confessed and implicated a fellow gang member, Pan Rongmu. Stolen goods were also found at the home of Pan's relative, surnamed Jin. The suspects all admitted to robbing the Lu and Xu families and sharing the spoils without denying anything. The team is continuing to investigate and is expected to quell the banditry in Punan.

Wuxi: Total Grain Reserves in Eight Counties 71

The Second District Administrative Inspectorate of Jiangsu Province, acting on instructions from the provincial government, ordered the immediate dispatch of personnel to various counties to investigate the situation of grain reserves. Inspector Zang dispatched Adjutant Zhang Zhongli, Technician Wang Zipei, and Clerk Jing Tian to investigate the eight counties under its jurisdiction. The investigation has now been completed. It is estimated that the various warehouses in Wuxi store a total of 8,720 shi and 81 jin of grain, and the grain money is 3,836 yuan, 7 jiao, and several fen. The various warehouses in Wu County store a total of 157,764 shi and 86 jin of grain, and the grain money is 1,936 yuan, 1 jiao, and 9 fen. Wujiang stores 8,370 shi and 40 jin of grain, Kunshan stores 13,733 shi and 54 jin of grain, and the grain money is 55,171 yuan, 2 jiao, 4 fen, and 8 li. Taicang stores 19,105 shi and 96 jin of grain, and the grain money is 19,231 yuan, 6 jiao, and 6 fen. Changshu stores 4,396 shi of grain, and the grain money is 96,536 yuan, 7 jiao, and 3 fen. Wujin stores 50,063 shi and 81 jin of grain, 294 shi and 50 jin of wheat, and the grain money is 78,830 yuan, 2 jiao, 9 fen, and 6 li. Jiangyin stores 19,349 shi and 55 jin of grain, and the grain money is 34,348 yuan, 7 jiao, 7 fen, and 1 li. The above grain reserves and grain money shall be properly kept by the various counties and shall not be used without authorization.

Capture of Chao Lake Bandit Gang 72

Wu Shaozhi, the head of the Fourth Regiment of the Local Militia Defense Corps in this county, recently received confidential information from informants stating that six or seven bandits from the Chao Lake gang, including Xia Zichang, were hiding on a boat near Wuqiao outside the North Gate, intending to commit robbery. He requested the immediate dispatch of a team to apprehend them. Upon receiving the report, Director Wu, yesterday (the 27th) around 4:00 AM, led Special Agent Wang Julin, regiment adjutants Wu Baishun and Xia Fengchang, and detectives Dai Quan and Wang Shuanglin from the Public Security Bureau to search and arrest them. They successfully captured a large rice barge at Shuanghekou and apprehended bandits Xia Zichang, Xia Tianxi, Xia Fangping, and Chen Shunjiao. They also seized one No. 3 box cannon, thirty rounds of ammunition, and one six-inch pistol with five rounds of ammunition. All were sent to the Public Security Bureau for custody. It is reported that the bandits are related to robbery cases in Beizhakou and the Zhu Zhan Alley on Changan Bridge.

The Zhenjiang County Opium Prohibition Committee is actively promoting voluntary surrender for opium offenders. With only five days remaining until the deadline for voluntary surrender, in addition to intensifying publicity and warnings, yesterday they also purchased ten coffins and placed them in various important traffic locations, with warning slogans posted on them, in order to prompt opium offenders to quickly awaken, surrender voluntarily, avoid the clutches of the law, and serve as a warning. It is reported that more than fifty opium offenders from various villages and towns have voluntarily surrendered in recent days.

Jiashan: Zhonghu Ferry Robbed Again 74

The Lixing ferry on the Shenhu route was robbed by bandits in October. The perpetrators, Zhang Sanbao and two others, were just arrested on the 18th in Wuzhen and Zhenze and handed over to the authorities. Unexpectedly, at midnight on the 23rd, in the area of Qiandun Port in this county, they were robbed again by a gang of more than twenty bandits who boarded three boats, blocked the ferry, and fired dozens of shots. The drivers, sailors, and passengers on board were all bound and allowed to be looted at will, resulting in losses of more than three thousand yuan. Zhu Liangwu, the captain of the county's water and land regiment police, led the water police team to pursue the bandits.

The Fourth District Commissioner inspected Haimen on the 26th and proceeded to Qidong. He returned to Tong on the 31st. On New Year's Day, he inspected the water and land public security teams at the public sports field.

Ningbo: Aftermath of the Chunyu Bank Debt 76

Since the sudden collapse of the Chunyu Bank in the Western Suburbs in 1933, it has accumulated debts of more than 200,000 yuan. After years of litigation, a solution is gradually being reached. However, a few creditors, including Fan Feng, represented by Chen Maochang, hired lawyer Chen Hanru to file a lawsuit of objection. After mediation by the execution court failed, Fan and others sued Chen Maochang at the prosecutor's office for colluding with depositors and forging meeting minutes for a 20% repayment agreement, damaging the rights of other creditors. The prosecutor's office accepted the complaint and once summoned Chen for questioning, ordering Chen to provide cash bail pending trial.

Taixian: Prison and Detention Center Plan to Establish Factories 77

The capacity of the prison and detention center in this county was originally set at 400 inmates. Recently, due to a sharp increase in opium-related cases, the number of detainees and convicts in both places has reached more than 600, exceeding the original capacity by more than half, resulting in extreme overcrowding. Ye Chengshu, the warden of the prison and concurrently the director of the detention center, has submitted a request to the county government for permission to alleviate the situation through bail and parole. However, after a recent investigation, the number of inmates in the prison and detention center who meet the requirements for parole is very small. It is now proposed to allocate a portion of the inmates to learn crafts in order to alleviate the overcrowding. The search for factory locations is currently underway and is expected to be realized soon.

Enthusiastic Support for the Suiyuan Campaign 78

Since hearing about the outbreak of the Suiyuan War, all sectors of this county have been unusually excited. In addition to various schools, districts, villages, and government agencies spontaneously organizing donation groups to support the Suiyuan campaign in various places, the county party headquarters and the county government have also convened all sectors to establish the "County-wide Promotion of One-Day Donation Campaign and Comforting Suiyuan Soldiers Donation Committee" to solicit donations from all parties. Recently, the businesses in the city area, the Tailai Flour Mill, the money shop industry, and other merchants have responded to the one-day donation campaign. Other donations are also being coordinated by Cao Deliang, the director of solicitation of the committee.

Xiaoshan: Land Survey Renamed Land Administration 79

The Xiaoshan Land Survey Office is scheduled to be reorganized into the Land Administration Office on New Year's Day in 1937. The original General Affairs Section will be renamed the First Section, and the Map and Photo Section will be renamed the Second Section. Internal staff will be kept in their existing positions as much as possible to ensure familiarity with the work. In addition, the Sha Tian Affairs Office of the Sha Tian Commissioner, which was abolished and merged into the Sha Tian Section of the Second Division of the County Government, will also be transferred to the Land Administration Office for management.

Refugees Disturbing Villages 80

On the 25th, more than 200 refugees arrived in Anchang, Guali, and other places bordering Shaoxing and Xiaoshan. They disturbed the villages in the area and occupied the Jiudun Temple. The Anchang Public Security Sub-bureau, together with the Security Team, rushed to the area to intercept and drive them out.

Random Notes from a Trip to Europe (2) 81

— Our Correspondent in Europe, Lieshan

6. Being a Foreign Correspondent

Mr. Rosenberg, the Minister of the Foreign Political Department of the German National Socialist Party, is one of the most important theorists of National Socialism (often referred to as Hitlerism by foreign newspapers). His books are not only good materials for us to study National Socialism, but he is also said to be a key figure in charge of German foreign policy. He often hosts guests once a month, and each time there is a speech by a famous member of the National Socialist Party. The people invited are all foreign diplomats and journalists stationed in Germany. One time, the speaker was Mr. Lutze, the Supreme Commander of the National Socialist Party's Stormtroopers (SA). Mr. Lutze's speech mainly explained that the current instability in the world is the result of Jewish, Communist, and Soviet Russian troublemaking, and he expressed Germany's sincere efforts to safeguard world peace. Although we often hear his arguments in Germany and do not find them particularly novel, the audience that day was foreign diplomats and journalists, and many of them were of Jewish descent. For example, sitting next to me was the German correspondent for the Soviet Russian newspaper Pravda, who happened to be the target of Mr. Lutze's attack that day: Jews, Communists, and Soviet Russian nationals. Although that correspondent was present during Mr. Lutze's speech, he remained calm throughout, with no expression on his face, and only kept smoking cigarettes desperately. Later, I secretly asked him for his thoughts, and he said, "What else can I do? I'm used to it and don't feel anything." Then I thought of the experiences of German journalists in Moscow.

A British journalist said, "Sir, don't just worry about the 'colleagues' from Germany and Russia. In fact, the most pitiful are we foreign correspondents from 'democratic' countries. We don't know if we will be expelled tomorrow. The guarantee our country gives us is just a piece of empty paper of protest. Germany and Russia are dictatorships. If the German government expels a Russian journalist today, Moscow will immediately be missing a German journalist tomorrow. So journalists from these two countries dare to attack each other's weaknesses as much as possible without any scruples. They are the ones to be envied. Like us, we can only be worried every day!"

7. A Female Journalist

Since the German National Socialist Party came to power and Dr. Goebbels became the Minister of Propaganda, foreign journalists stationed in Germany have found it particularly difficult to gather news. There are two main sources for ordinary foreign correspondents to gather news: referring to local newspapers. However, after all German newspapers have been checked by the Propaganda Department, it is not easy to find any special materials there. All important political news is published simultaneously by all newspapers at the time designated by the authorities. In this way, German journalists are unable to develop their personal talents directly. Indirectly, foreign journalists stationed in Germany are also being affected. Secondly, frequent interactions with local people. In recent years, due to political reasons, the interactions between ordinary Germans and foreign journalists have gradually decreased. This point has become a fatal injury for foreign journalists stationed in Germany. Except for a few famous journalists, everyone is gradually finding it difficult to make a living. Although there is still one exception.

A few months ago, in the days before Germany was about to march into the Rhineland, rumors spread in Berlin that there would be a major event. Foreign journalists naturally went out to inquire, hoping to immediately report on this news. However, everyone wasted a lot of effort, and in the end, they only found out after the German official announcement was issued. Only one Polish female reporter actually obtained all the news twenty-four hours before the advance. She immediately telegraphed this news to Warsaw. As a result, this Polish newspaper was the first newspaper in the world to publish this news. After reading the report, the Polish Ministry of Foreign Affairs telegraphed the Polish ambassador in Berlin to inquire about the truth of the German advance into the Rhineland. It can be seen that the German government kept this news very secret in the diplomatic world.

In Europe, female reporters are not highly valued. People in the journalism industry also have this view. This time, the female reporter actually created a new record in such a difficult situation. We can imagine her pride. Later, I told this story to an acquaintance. He said, "Humph! It's a female reporter, of course! I said: Brother, you can't misunderstand. I know her, she is a middle-aged woman in her forties or fifties."

8. London Newspapers

British politicians like to say that the British navy is the best in the world, the army is also the best in the world, and the air force will soon be the best in the world. Reuters has been actively promoting this view in Chinese newspapers. The reason is very simple. British colonies are all over the world. Since other people are unwilling to say so, then we have to come forward ourselves.

A month ago, former British Prime Minister MacDonald, as usual, said at the British Journalists' Association that British newspapers are the best in the world. Even if Mr. MacDonald didn't say this, we would also like to promote it for it. British newspapers not only deserve this honor in terms of editing, printing, and circulation, but they have also become a tool for educating the public. Most importantly, reading newspapers has become a part of people's daily lives. Whether on trains, subways, or buses, you can almost see every passenger with a newspaper. From the far-right newspaper, the Mail, to the far-left communist organ, the Daily Worker, from the dignified Times to the Sunday papers read by carters and maids, such as the News of the World (which has a circulation of 3.35 million copies), there are all kinds. In this process, you can easily choose a newspaper to read according to your taste. Or reading several newspapers at the same time will not make you feel dry, because each newspaper has its own special features. In the UK, an ordinary box of cigarettes is priced at six old pence, while each newspaper only costs one penny.

JINAN FOOTBALL DECLINES RAPIDLY; LOST TO WESTERN MERCHANTS 4-1 YESTERDAY; FIRST HALF UNILATERALLY BECAME 3-1 84

Jinan and Western Merchants met again yesterday at Shen Garden for the second round of the West League A Group football match, competing for the fourth place. Jinan had rallied briefly in the middle of last month, but the good times did not last long, and recently it has felt like its performance is declining rapidly. Yesterday, Wang Nanzhen was absent due to the Iron City Cup basketball game in the evening, and Yin Guiren was also absent at the same time. Ye Peichu was also absent due to exams, making the lineup even more sparse.

First Half

As a result, Western Merchants had the advantage of the sun at their backs and the wind at their sails. Although Jinan took the initiative, they were quickly intercepted, and at the same time, their own territory was in danger. After holding on for seven minutes, Western Merchant's left winger, Allison, crossed the ball from the baseline, hitting Xu Hongyin, who deflected it into his own net, opening the scoring. After that, Jinan repeatedly encountered dangerous situations, but fortunately, the defense was effective and they did not concede again. However, the situation was still controlled by Western Merchants. Jinan only managed to get one scoring opportunity with great difficulty, and won a free kick 15 yards out. Although Zhang Riyuan's kick was good, Cai Daojin was a step too late and missed the chance. When 34 minutes had passed, Allison attacked again, and Yifu Glai Fu received the ball that De Luse missed between his legs and scored with one touch, giving Western Merchants a two-goal lead. Jinan fought back vigorously, and about four minutes before the break, Cai Daojin advanced along the wing and crossed the ball. Pei Yongnan shot from 15 yards out, pulling back one goal. However, two minutes later, Guan Jiyang mistakenly committed a handball, and a penalty was awarded. Jack scored the penalty, giving Western Merchants a 3-1 lead at halftime.

Second Half

After the restart, Jinan had the advantage of favorable terrain, but heaven did not help them, and the wind stopped suddenly, causing their sluggish feet to fail to take advantage of the wind. Xue Yongyuan, Wu Shufen, Shi Yongnan, and others had several good chances, but they were all saved by the two defenders of Western Merchants one by one. Although the attack intensified, all their efforts were in vain. After 17 minutes, Western Merchants launched a large-scale attack, and the area in front of Jinan's goal was chaotic. Yifu Glai Fu took advantage of the situation and scored with one shot, securing the victory with a 4-1 lead. Afterwards, although Jinan still tried their best to attack, with Chen Zhenxiang moved forward to charge, they ultimately failed to achieve anything. However, when Wu Shufen advanced to about five yards from the opponent's goal, Gilbert Meng desperately rushed out to save, but Wu's hard foot unfortunately hit Gilbert's lower abdomen. The ball was saved, but the person also fell to the ground injured. The match was temporarily suspended, and Western Merchants replaced their left forward Moore with a goalkeeper, while Gilbert Meng temporarily went out to rest. Fortunately, after a few minutes, he recovered and barely managed to hold on until the end of the game, which ended with a 4-1 victory for Western Merchants. According to the first time Jinan met Western Merchants, they also lost 2-1, so Western Merchants should have a greater advantage in the future development, and Western Merchants can generally stand out in the fourth place. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

WESTERN YOUTH BASKETBALL TONIGHT 85

Nanjing, Central News Agency, 27th - The cross-country race organized by the Beijing University Sports Association started at 10:00 AM on the 27th outside Zhongshan Gate, at Wei Bridge, and returned to the original site via Huanling Road and the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, a total distance of approximately 8,000 meters. COLLEGE AND MIDDLE SCHOOL STUDENTS PARTICIPATE IN CELEBRATION OF CHAIRMAN JIANG'S RETURN TO NANJING ASSEMBLY; ASSEMBLY HELD TODAY AT 2:00 PM; MUNICIPAL SOCIAL BUREAU HAS ISSUED NOTICES FOR COMPLIANCE 92

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau has issued a notice regarding the participation of college and middle school students in Shanghai in the Shanghai citizens' celebration of Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing: The Shanghai citizens' celebration of Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing will be held at 2:00 PM on the 28th of this month (Monday) at the Nanshi Daji Road Public Sports Field. All universities and middle schools in Shanghai South District 1, Shanghai South District 2, Special District 1, and Special District 2 will suspend classes for half a day on that afternoon, and each school will designate two marshals and commanders to lead all students to the field to participate before 1:30 PM. Universities and middle schools in Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, and Pudong districts should contact the party headquarters in their respective districts for arrangements. If a half-day suspension of classes is required, it will be approved. Now, the measures for participating in the celebration have been stipulated, and a copy of the measures is attached for compliance. This notice is hereby issued. A copy of the measures is attached. December 27th, 25th year of the Republic of China, Director Gong Zhan.

Participation Measures

1. Date: December 28th (Monday) at 2:00 PM sharp. 2. Location: Nanshi Public Sports Field. 3. Assembly order: (1) Music and opening ceremony, (2) Singing the Party song, (3) Paying the highest respect to the national flag and the portrait of the Premier, (4) Reading the Premier's last will, (5) Silence, (6) Report, (7) Speech. 4. Slogans: (1) Long live Chairman Chiang, (2) Long live the Kuomintang, (3) Long live the Republic of China. 5. Parade. 6. Parade instructions: (1) All junior high school students from each school must wear boy scout uniforms, and all senior high school and university students must wear uniforms. Each person must hold a national flag. (2) Each school should designate one leader, one marshal, and one commander, and prepare one leader, one marshal, and one commander flag. They will listen to the assignments of the general marshals and general commanders of the assembly. 3. Each school must provide a large white bamboo cloth banner with the school name written on it. 4. Marshals and commanders of each school should lead the team in double columns. 5. Participants in the parade must complete the entire route.

MUNICIPAL PEOPLE'S EDUCATION HALL CELEBRATES CHAIRMAN'S SAFE RETURN; SCHOOLS HOLD CELEBRATIONS 93

The Municipal People's Education Hall on Wenmiao Road in this city held an expanded celebration at 10:00 AM the other day in the lecture hall of the hall to commemorate Chairman Jiang's return to Nanjing to take charge. More than a thousand people from all walks of life attended. The meeting was held in a burst of cheers by the director of the hall, Xu Zexiang. The chairman immediately reported on the revolutionary achievements of Chairman Jiang's life and the significance of the meeting. Then, he introduced Zheng Xigu, a famous figure in the education sector and the principal of the provincial Shanghai Middle School, to give a speech. Zheng, with a kind attitude and popular language, first talked about China's glorious history in the past, the difficult environment after the September 18th Incident, and Chairman Jiang's diligent governance in the past five years. He suddenly encountered the Xi'an Incident, and we are very heartbroken. Then he talked about the depth of the people's love and the efforts of the people to support Chairman Jiang during his time of hardship, so that the countries of the upper world knew that the Chinese government had a sound organization and a great leader to lead the people to work hard for national construction. Because of Chairman Jiang's great personality, he was able to escape from danger quickly this time. He said, after our leader Chairman Jiang escaped from danger, at the very least, we should have the following two understandings and efforts: (1) We should follow everything that Chairman Jiang has always shown us, be down-to-earth, take responsibility, and help the government gather national strength to seek the revival and strength of our nation; (2) We should clearly recognize what is right and wrong, distinguish between obedience and disobedience, not be confused by heresies, not be moved by villains, create true public opinion, and assist the government in suppressing rebels and wiping out heresies. Under the leadership of the only leader Chairman Jiang, the foundation of the country will be more stable, and the glorious Chinese nation that has been responsible for thousands of years will embark on the road to revival.

Daxia University, Daxia University held a celebration for Chairman Chiang's safe return at 10:30 AM yesterday, with 2,000 faculty and students attending. First, Vice President Ou, the chairman, delivered the opening remarks, followed by a chorus of patriotic songs to express congratulations, and then a speech by Dean of Academic Affairs Lu Jihui. Finally, firecrackers were set off and slogans such as "Support the leader who defends the country and repels foreign enemies" and "Support the policies of the central government" were shouted.

Chengdong Girls' School, Chengdong Girls' Middle School on Huayi Street, Nanshi, has always focused on teaching current affairs and training patriotic sentiments. After the news of Chairman Chiang's escape spread the other day, the school held a celebration performance last night in addition to joyfully celebrating. There were many programs, and the most exciting ones were Ge Fujuan's "Beautiful Night," Cheng Chunshi's "Butterfly Shoes," and Gong Xueheng and Cao Suping's "Loving Mother," which were fully rehearsed and performed with great spirit. The play "Awakening" featured Xu Xinbao performing the role of a genuine woman, which was quite heroic, and Gong Xueheng's portrayal of a bad young man was vivid and won a lot of applause. Cheng Qi's harmonica solo was just right, and the chorus of "Family" and "Storm on the Yangtze River" by the second-grade students excited the audience. The firecrackers of the previous night were followed by a solo by Xue Jinghua, a teacher at the school, and a Peking opera performance by Han Beiling, which was humorous and made people laugh.

Shanghai Girls' Middle School, Shanghai Girls' Middle School on Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road, Nanshi, burst into cheers and set off firecrackers to celebrate as soon as they received the news of Chairman Chiang's escape. A celebration for Chairman Chiang's escape was held on the afternoon of the other day during the weekly meeting at 2:00 PM. The head of discipline, Ms. Fu Xiaofeng, reported on the significance of the meeting, and teachers, staff, and workers from all levels performed.

Provincial Shanghai Middle School, After the teachers and students of the Provincial Shanghai Middle School heard the news of Chairman Jiang's escape the other night, they immediately convened a celebration meeting. Principal Zheng Tonghe officially reported to all teachers and students, who were overjoyed. After the meeting, firecrackers were set off, and Principal Zheng led the cheering slogans. Yesterday, a congratulatory telegram was sent to Chairman Chiang, which read: To Chairman Jiang in Luoyang, Yesterday evening, I learned that Chairman had flown to Luoyang, the country was rejoicing and celebrating together. This is a respectful offering. The entire faculty and students of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School respectfully kowtow.

Shanghai Business College, Upon learning of Chairman Chiang's escape, the students of the National Shanghai Business College were ecstatic, dancing and cheering, purchasing a large number of firecrackers to set off in celebration, the sound piercing the clouds, as if a great war had suddenly arrived. Then, they automatically reorganized and set out on a parade, led by the military band, the order solemn. Along the road, they chanted slogans such as "Long live Chairman Chiang," "Long live the Republic of China," and "Chairman Chiang is the savior of China," pedestrians stopping to watch, and residents responding to the sound, causing traffic jams. Upon reaching Two Jiangs Girls' School, the students of that school were already waiting in formation on the playground. Thereupon, they united and advanced to Fudan University, circling the school's football field once. Every time they reached a dormitory, they shouted, "Welcome Fudan students to join the celebration," and no fewer than hundreds of people responded. At this point, the three schools united, and the momentum grew even greater. Thousands of people continued to advance, passing Southeast Girls' Physical Education Teachers' School and Yuqing Middle School, before turning back to Fudan University and resting briefly in front of the gate. The students of that school then purchased a large number of firecrackers, which were set off by more than a dozen people in different places.

Tongji University, Tongji University sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang: To Chairman Chiang in Luoyang, Congratulations to the Chairman for safely arriving in Luoyang and preparing to return to the capital. The entire nation feels like they have seen the sun again. I am pleased to report that amidst the cheers of the masses, Weng Zhilong, President of National Tongji University, and all faculty, staff, and students respectfully kowtow and ask for forgiveness.

Huadong Girls' Middle School, The entire faculty and students of Huadong Girls' Middle School on Xia Road in this city were extremely saddened and indignant after Chairman Chiang was kidnapped. They were very excited to hear the news of the leader's escape. It is reported that the school will hold a teachers and students' party starting at 9:00 AM today (the 27th) to express its congratulations and enthusiasm for protecting the leader. In addition to the fun dramas performed by each grade, there are also various programs such as Kunqu opera and dance.

MEASURES TO MAINTAIN EFFECTIVE USE OF RADIOS ANNOUNCED BY THE MINISTRY OF EDUCATION 94

The Ministry of Education formulated and announced the measures to maintain the effective use of radios on the 26th. The original text is as follows: (1) The education halls and bureaus in each province and city should, in accordance with the provisions of item 3 of the broadcasting education implementation measures issued by the Ministry, quickly delineate broadcasting education guidance areas and appoint graduates of the Ministry's electrical education training class to serve as guidance officers in each area. (2) Each broadcasting area should establish a radio repair center so that it can be repaired at any time when parts are damaged. However, for provinces and cities with a small number of radio stations, a repair center may be established within the hall or bureau, and repair tools should be purchased to carry out repairs. The purchase of these repair tools should be paid for by the education halls and bureaus of each province and city to the Ministry for ordering from various factories on their behalf (each set of radio repair tools costs 210 yuan). However, the Ministry may provide subsidies to remote and poor provinces. If the professional personnel who repair radios, such as the electrical education personnel who have been sent by the provinces and cities to the Ministry for training, are not qualified due to insufficient academic qualifications, the education halls and bureaus of each province and city may first select one or two of the best-educated among them and report them to the Ministry. The Ministry will transfer them to major electrical machinery factories for internships. The internship period is temporarily set at two months. During the internship period, the original service unit will continue to pay the original salary on a monthly basis. (3) When the radios in each school or library in each province and city cannot receive sound or encounter other obstacles, they should immediately report to the broadcasting education guidance area to which they belong for repair. (4) If the parts are too badly damaged to be repaired, they may be sent by the education halls and bureaus of each province and city to the Ministry for replacement with a new machine. The round-trip transportation costs will be borne by the original radio station, but the Ministry may provide subsidies to remote and poor provinces. (5) The dry batteries prepared for DC radios can usually only be used for two or three months. After that, new batteries must be purchased. Each frame radio must purchase new dry batteries at least four times a year. The purchase of these dry batteries should be based on a comprehensive calculation of the number of dry batteries that need to be replaced for all the radios installed in the schools and libraries in the province and city, and the purchase should be ordered in large quantities from the Ministry, and the cost of each set of dry batteries, 19 yuan and 6 jiao, should be paid at one time, so that they can be purchased from the Construction Committee's Lei Machinery Factory. (6) The Ministry may consider providing subsidies to schools and libraries in remote and poor provinces that need dry batteries. (7) If the education halls and bureaus of each province and city and each school or library have any questions about the situation of radios, they can directly ask the broadcasting education committee of the Ministry.

Citywide Flag Hanging Today to Celebrate Chairman Chiang's Return to Nanjing; Citizen's Congress and Grand Parade to be Held 105

To be held at the Public Stadium at 2 PM; All Sectors Held Preparatory Meeting Yesterday to Decide Everything; Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Industries to Send Representatives to Participate; Flying Club Sends Two Airplanes to Distribute Slogans

Since Chairman Chiang's safe arrival in Luoyang and return to Nanjing, the emotions of the citizens of this city have been extremely jubilant. The municipal party and government organs, in order to ensure that the citizens can unanimously express their feelings, have decided to hold a Shanghai citizens' celebration congress at the Public Stadium in the South City at 2 PM today (the 28th) to celebrate Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing, and to hold a grand parade. The four districts of Pudong, Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong will also hold separate events at the same time. Yesterday (the 27th) at 10 AM, the municipal party headquarters convened a preparatory meeting of representatives from various organs in the conference room of the headquarters to make slight modifications to the parade route and order. The Social Affairs Bureau ordered all major middle schools to take a half-day holiday to participate. The decided-upon measures and the meeting's proceedings are recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives

Those present yesterday included Tao Baichuan and Lu Jingshi from the municipal party headquarters; Wang Daxu from the Social Affairs Bureau; Chen Xiaomei from the Ninth District Party Headquarters; Zhang Wenshan from the Fourth District Party Headquarters; Shi Zizhi from the Special Party Headquarters of the Security Corps; Feng Guangjia from the Third District Party Headquarters; Lu Nan from the Security Corps Headquarters; Wang Weiming from the Public Security Bureau; Liu Yuwen from the Military Training Association; Li Jianbai from the Seamen's Union; Li Dachao from the Municipal Government; Bao Henian from the First District Party Headquarters; Feng Xiancheng from the Sixth District Party Headquarters; Zhu Yuanhui from the Security Committee; Huang Xianggu from the Second Special District Citizens' Association; Yuan Hongjun from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Huang Yanpei from the Local Association; Shen Yu from the Fifth District Party Headquarters; Yu Yaoqiu from the First Special District Citizens' Association; Fan Wei from the Garrison Command; Zhu Xuefan from the General Labor Union; Huang Zaoxiong (Zhang on behalf) from the Municipal Education Association; Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers' Association; Pang Jingzhou from the Red Cross Society; Diao Qingen from the Seventh District Party Headquarters; Wang Tongde from the Tenth District Party Headquarters; Wang Manyun from the Lawyers' Association; and Wu Zhen from the Second District Party Headquarters, totaling more than twenty people.

Discussion Measures

Chairman Tao Baichuan presided, Du Mengsen recorded. After the meeting commenced as scheduled, Chairman Tao first reported, stating that since the various sectors of this city heard of Chairman Chiang's safe arrival, the emotions of the masses have been extraordinarily jubilant. The municipal party and government organs, in order to ensure that the emotions of all citizens are expressed uniformly, have specifically proposed convening a citizens' congress and parade measures, etc. Then, the draft measures were proposed, amended, and passed, and it was decided that all major middle schools in the city would be given a half-day holiday today (the 28th), to be notified by the Social Affairs Bureau. At the same time, Lu Jingshi was appointed as the general commander of the parade, and Wang Weiming was appointed as the general inspector of the parade. The measures are recorded as follows: (1) Convene the Shanghai citizens' celebration congress for Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing; (2) Date: 2 PM on the 28th of this month; (3) Location: Public Stadium in the South City.

Congress Staff

(A) The presidium will be composed of representatives from the following organs and groups: (1) Wu Kaixian from the Municipal Party Headquarters; (2) Mayor Wu from the Municipal Government; (3) Commander Yang from the Garrison Command; (4) Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers' Association; (5) Zhu Xuefan from the General Labor Union; (6) Wang Xiaolai from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; (7) Huang Zaoxiong from the Municipal Education Association; (8) Jiang Huaisu from the Security Committee; (9) Li Xiangqi from the Civil Training Office; (10) Tong Xingbai from the Boy Scouts Council; (11) Du Yuesheng from the Local Association; (12) Shi Zizhi from the Security Party Headquarters; (13) Wang Jiyi from the Seamen's Union; (14) Lin Kanghou from the Citizens' Federation; (15) Wang Xiaoying from the women's sector. (B) Master of ceremonies: Zhang Hanyun; Recorders: Tong Muge, Du Mengsen; Reception: Huang Xianggu, Huang E, Zhu Xiaochun, Wu Xianren, Li Baiqing, Cao Runsen, Guo Mingting, Yan Kezong, Bao Huizhong, etc. (C) Security personnel will be jointly provided by the Garrison Command, the Security Corps, the Public Security Bureau, and the Security Committee.

Congress Order

(1) Music and opening; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Pay the highest respect to the national flag, the Party flag, and the portrait of the Premier; (4) Respectfully read the Premier's will; (5) Silence; (6) Report; (7) Speech; (8) Discuss proposals; (9) Shout slogans; (10) Adjournment; (11) Parade. Parade Measures

(7) Parade route: Depart from the northwest corner gate of the venue, go north on Fangxie Road to Laoximen, turn onto Zhonghua Road, then Minguo Road, and disperse at Heping Road in Laoximen.

Parade Instructions

(1) Participants must arrive at the Public Stadium by 1:30 PM; (2) (A) 1. Police, 2. Trainee citizens, enter the venue through the Fangxie Road gate; (B) 1. Security corps, 2. Other citizens (including farmers, industry, and commerce groups and representatives of various organs), enter the venue through the Dalin Road gate; (C) 1. Security team, 2. Students and Boy Scouts, enter the venue through the Daji Road gate; (3) Participants must each carry a small national flag, to be provided by the participants themselves; (4) Pilgrims must appoint one leader and one inspector-commander for every hundred people, who will be subject to the direction of the general inspector and general commander of the congress parade team; (5) Participants must prepare a large white cloth banner stating the organ or group they represent, and the inspector-commander must prepare two flags; (6) When entering the venue, participants should gather at the venue designated by the general commander of the congress; (7) When starting the parade, each inspector-commander should order the team they lead to advance in a double-file column; (8) Participants must complete the entire parade route.

(9) Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, and Pudong districts, due to distance, the municipal party headquarters will order the party headquarters in each region to hold a celebration meeting on the same day in conjunction with various political and military sectors.
