Celebratory Meetings Held Yesterday by Various Circles: Celebrating Chairman Chiang's Return to Nanjing 106

Two Railway Party Branches

The Special Party Branch of the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, on the occasion of Chairman Chiang's safe return to the capital, specially convened the party members of the railway yesterday in the railway bureau auditorium to hold a celebratory meeting for Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing. More than a thousand colleagues from various departments attended. At the start of the celebration, they first sang the Party Song and the Leader's Song. Then, Chairman Chen Chengshi respectfully read the Premier's testament. Following this, Chairman Li Dasan reported on the significance of the celebration, with the gist as follows: "Today's celebration of Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing is of great significance. First, the greatness of the leader's personality: in Xi'an, he faced adversity, unyielding in the face of coercion, placing life and death aside. Second, Zhang Xueliang and others, incited by treacherous individuals, staged a rebellion, but after reading the leader's diary, they were deeply moved by his sincerity, suddenly awakened, and respectfully escorted the leader back to Nanjing to exercise his duties. We know that the leader's captivity was the crisis of the Chinese nation. Today, the leader's safe return to Nanjing is the glory of national revival. From now on, we should continue to work hard, be loyal to the Party and the nation, support the leader, and abide by the Premier's teachings to achieve the goal of China's independence, freedom, and equality," and so on. After that, Railway Bureau representative Secretary Fan Shouzhi, Chief of the Xiao Transportation Office Wei Guo, Party Branch Standing Committee member Chen Chengshi, and Secretary-General Shi Guoyuan delivered speeches in succession. After shouting slogans, the entire group went downstairs, took a photo in front of the gate, and then dispersed.

Security Teams

The Party Affairs Guidance Committee convened representatives from subordinate party branches and teams yesterday to hold an enthusiastic celebration of Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing. More than three hundred and fifty representatives from party branches and teams attended. The meeting was originally chaired by Mayor Wu, who also served as a committee member, but due to Mayor Wu's important official duties, Committee member Shi Ziya took over as chairman. He led the attendees in performing the rituals as required and delivered a report on the spot, stating briefly, "Since the leader's misfortune, the people of the country have been filled with worry and indignation. This is because Chairman Chiang's safety is the safety of the nation and the country. Fortunately, Heaven has blessed China, and Chairman Chiang has safely arrived in Nanjing to exercise his duties. In the future, our nation and country will once again advance under the leadership of Chairman Chiang towards the three paths of independence, freedom, and equality. The bright and splendid future is foreseeable. My comrades and compatriots, from now on, should redouble our efforts, adhere to the leader's national salvation ideas, and eliminate national difficulties. This is why I wish our leader had experienced such hardship for the sake of the country, suffering several days of confinement, but his military duty was also irreproachable," and so on. Then, Deputy Commander Hua Zhou of the General Regiment gave a speech, stating briefly, "Since Chairman Chiang's misfortune, social order has been well-maintained, and the whole country has responded calmly. Ultimately, through the inspiration of Chairman Chiang's great personality, and the expression of the collective strength of the people, he escaped danger and came to Nanjing. This demonstrates that our country's organizational strength has been enhanced. By using this strength to save the country, what country cannot be saved? I hope that our compatriots will learn from this experience, and, without being idle or slack, under the leadership of our leader, unite sincerely, and move forward in unison. The day of light will not be far away," and so on. Then, they shouted slogans, and the resounding cheers shook the sky. The joyful scene is hard to describe with words.

Our labor circles deeply feel that Chairman Chiang's leadership has been effective and should celebrate even more. Now that Chairman Chiang has safely arrived in the capital and Zhang Xueliang has also come along, it is evident that he has indeed shown a determination to repent. The central government can grant him a lenient punishment. The Shanghai City Party Branch has specially decided to convene a citizens' assembly tomorrow to celebrate Chairman Chiang's escape from danger. As for the method, it will be reported by Standing Committee member Ye Xianggao of this union." He added, "Now that foreign insults are becoming increasingly urgent, the only person who can lead the nation's revival and liberate the workers is Chairman Chiang, who can shoulder this heavy responsibility. Therefore, we can only support the leader to revive the Republic of China and liberate the suffering of the workers. The purpose of today's meeting is to celebrate Chairman Chiang's escape from danger, his continued governance, and the revival of the Chinese nation," and so on. Then, Standing Committee member Ye Xianggao reported on the method of the citizens' assembly to be convened by the City Party Branch tomorrow, hoping that the workers would enthusiastically participate to show the enthusiasm of our labor circles in supporting the leader. Subsequently, Standing Committee member Shao Xubai gave a speech, stating briefly, "Since our supreme leader encountered misfortune in Xi'an, the people across the country have been shocked, as the country was in the midst of unification and resistance against the enemy was just beginning, encountering such a great disaster has placed the country in a critical situation. In addition to requesting the central government to punish the rebels, the Shanghai labor circles have also convened a labor circles discussion meeting to discuss maintaining local order. During these fourteen days, although there were some disputes, they were resolved immediately through the mediation of the Party and government. This proves that the workers have recognized the seriousness of the situation and are willing to step back to maintain order. Furthermore, the same calm response and adaptability of business circles and others are sufficient to prove the increased awareness of the people across the country. When the news of Chairman Chiang's escape from danger arrived, the enthusiastic emotions of the people from all walks of life were unprecedented, which is even more sufficient to prove the enthusiasm of the people in supporting the leader. We dare to say that this situation is no less than that of Hitler in Germany and Mussolini in Italy. From this incident, it can be seen that the strength of the Chinese people has been fully demonstrated. Our country has transformed from scattered sand into unity and from disorganized to organized. We firmly believe that under the leadership of Chairman Chiang, the country will not be difficult to revive and the lost territories will not be difficult to recover," and so on. In addition, the Yongjin Society, organized by the city's labor circles, and all the workers undergoing training held celebrations separately in the courtyards of their factories after receiving the news of Chairman Chiang's escape from danger. At the same time, in order to express its support for the leader, the society decided to convene a general assembly on New Year's Day of the 26th year of the Republic of China to hold a grand celebration.

Records of Current Events 108

Wu Tiecheng and Chen Zhaoying took the night train to Nanjing yesterday.

Page 10

Eurasia's Detained Airplane: Flew Back to Shanghai Yesterday from Shaanxi: Carrying Chen Cheng and Others Back to Nanjing, Chiang Fang Came to Shanghai: Pilot Celebrates Safety and Recounts the Experience 109

The Junkers aircraft No. 15 of Eurasia Aviation Corporation, which was detained in Xi'an, departed from Xi'an at 8:40 AM yesterday, carrying government officials Chen Cheng, Jiang Zuobin, Chen Jicheng, Qian Dajun, Wei Lihuang, Wan Yaohuang, Chen Diaoyuan, Zhu Shaoliang, Jiang Fangzhen, Jiang Xiaozhong, Section Chief Shao, and others, a total of eleven people. It stopped briefly in Zhengzhou around noon and arrived in Nanjing at 2:00 PM. Except for Jiang Fangzhen, who came to Shanghai on the same plane, all others disembarked in Nanjing.

Pilot Celebrates Airplane's Return to Shanghai

The airplane departed from Nanjing at 2:10 PM. According to the scheduled itinerary, it could have arrived at Longhua Airport at 4:00 PM in the afternoon. However, the pilot had been trapped in Xi'an for two weeks, and he was very happy to return to Shanghai safely. He specially flew around the city three times to mark the celebration. It finally landed at the airport at 4:25 PM. At that time, the company personnel were all at the airport to welcome them and extended their sympathy to the pilot and mechanics. They also opened champagne in the airport office to show their appreciation. The pilot, Ross, the mechanic, Fei Xier, and the telegraph operator all raised their glasses and drank heartily. However, each person had been trapped for more than ten days and had not shaved for a long time, and their short beards were disheveled. Amidst the joyful expression, their appearance was very comical.

Recounting the Situation at the Time of the Incident

The Xin Xin News Agency reporter rushed to the airport in advance to wait. According to the person in charge of managing the cargo on the plane, when the incident occurred, it was around 8:00 PM on the 11th. Gunshots were heard, starting sparsely and becoming dense. At that time, they only felt panic and confusion and did not understand what was happening. Only at dawn did they learn that an incident had occurred. Zhang Xueliang's soldiers stationed at the airport had already killed several people. However, the exact situation was still unclear because the airport was heavily guarded and completely isolated from the outside world, making it impossible to inquire about the facts. After several days, due to food shortages, the pilot negotiated and obtained several bags of flour. On the 25th, they learned that the incident had been resolved. The machinery of the airplane at Xi'an Airport had not been damaged, so there were no losses.

Jiang Fang Returns to Shanghai on the Airplane

Jiang Fangzhen, a famous veteran of the army, took a plane from Nanjing to Xi'an on the 11th of this month, originally to report to Chairman Chiang on his visit to various European countries for inspection. Unexpectedly, he encountered the incident and was also detained. He returned to Shanghai on the plane yesterday. After meeting with Jiang at the airport, the Xin Xin News Agency reporter went to visit his private residence on Guofu Men Road. According to him, when the incident occurred on the night of the 11th, he heard sparse gunshots at the Xijing Guest House and did not mind them. He still slept soundly. The next morning, the mutinous soldiers entered the guest house to search, and only then did he understand. Mr. Shao Yuanchong suddenly fled that night and was shot dead by the mutinous soldiers. Mr. Shao Lizi's wife was injured. The rumor that she had passed away is not accurate. This morning, he left Shaanxi and returned to Shanghai on the Eurasia airplane, designated by government order.

It is also reported that the company's regular flight No. 17 Junkers arrived in Shanghai at 6:15 PM last night. According to information obtained by the Xin Sheng News Agency, the generals who were detained in Shaanxi, Qian Dajun, Mao Bangchu, and others, totaling fifteen people, took this plane south. They disembarked when the plane passed through Nanjing, and none of them came to Shanghai on it.

Charity Organizations' Relief Association: Sent Telegrams to Overseas Chinese: Appealing for Relief of the Suiyuan War Disaster 110

The Shanghai Charity Organizations Joint Relief Association has decided to use the 100,000 public bonds allocated by the Ministry of Finance and the 20,000 yuan raised by the association and has dispatched Qu Wenliu, Yang Zigong, and Feng Yangshan to Suiyuan to investigate and distribute relief to the disaster victims. They have also sent telegrams to our country's ambassadors and consuls in various countries to publicize the relief efforts and solicit donations from overseas Chinese. At the same time, they have also telegraphed overseas chambers of commerce, requesting their donations. The two telegrams are recorded below: (Telegram 1) (Title omitted) Acknowledgment, the bandits and puppets have invaded the border. Fortunately, the soldiers have bravely fought and repeatedly defeated the fierce enemies. You must be delighted to hear of this. However, to resist aggression, we must be able to sustain it. To make the soldiers fight bravely and invigorate the national spirit, it is especially important to ensure that the people in the war zone are not displaced and can fulfill their rear service. Chen Zhaoying Discusses Rapid Progress of Fujian Province People, Love for Country and Leader, Taking Pride in Using National Products 112

Mr. Chen Zhaoying, Inspector of Zhejiang and Fujian Provinces, flew from Fujian to Shanghai yesterday and stayed at Mr. Zhang's residence on Moore Road. He is scheduled to take the night train to Beijing at 11 o'clock last night to report to the Central Government on the recent situation in Fujian Province and the process of his inspection tour in eastern Fujian. A reporter from the Central News Agency met with Mr. Chen yesterday afternoon and had the following conversation:

Progress of the People

According to Mr. Chen, since the Xi'an Incident, Fujian Province has been quite peaceful. Although the financial circles were extremely nervous for two days, the 13th and 14th, they quickly stabilized. This is because the people learned that Chairman Chiang was safe in Shaanxi and were deeply convinced that he would be out of danger soon. In recent years, the people have made rapid progress and have a deep understanding of the country and the leader, regarding the leader's freedom as their own freedom and the leader's safety as their own safety. On the 17th, Fujian Province received a telegram from Shanghai that falsely reported that Chairman Chiang had been in danger, and the people spontaneously set off firecrackers to celebrate, spending as much as 30,000 yuan. On the 25th, when they learned that Chairman Chiang had safely arrived in Luoyang, the people were overjoyed and set off firecrackers, spending as much as 100,000 yuan. This is enough to show the people's support for the government and their love for the leader. The effect of the government's usual training of the people is also manifested in this fact. I am deeply convinced that once the war of national survival breaks out, the people will be able to work together under the leadership of the government.

Recent Situation in Fujian Province

The Party, government, and military in Fujian Province can cooperate closely, and every movement and undertaking can be jointly promoted, with multiplied effects. During my inspection tour of various places in eastern Fujian, although the transportation is inconvenient, the people are also very progressive. Moreover, the people in several places are proud of using national products and ashamed of using foreign goods. Imported goods have completely disappeared. This phenomenon will be even more widespread in the future. The troops are making great efforts to suppress the remaining bandits in eastern Fujian, and it is expected that they can be wiped out within a month and a half. Recently, Fujian Province has been promoting the Baojia system, and the burden on the people is relatively heavy. The provincial government is currently planning to reduce it.

Returning to Beijing Soon

President Yu has been ordered to go to Shaanxi to express his condolences. It is said that he will leave for Beijing in a day or two. I will enter Beijing tonight (the 27th) and plan to stay in Beijing for a few days before transferring to Zhejiang to inspect the expansion of the Binshan Baisha Elementary School.

Supporting Suiyuan Fundraising Campaign

Binshan County Baisha Elementary School has achieved great results in the implementation of special education. On November 17th of this year, it held a fundraising event for the whole school to support Suiyuan. The donated funds were sent to this newspaper to be transferred to the front line. It is now known that the school recently implemented a Suiyuan support center training and, after class, united with all sectors of society to hold an expanded Suiyuan support fundraising campaign. Each team went to the Yangxing Town area to distribute leaflets and solicit donations from door to door. A total of 19.5 yuan was donated and has been sent to this newspaper to be transferred to the front line. It is also known that the school has printed the fundraising accounts and posted them on the streets to report to the donors.

Shanghai County Reduces and Exempts Land Taxes, Handled in Accordance with Regulations, County Government Public Notice 114

Since Shanghai County changed to collecting land value tax this year, all land with reduced and exempted taxes should be re-verified in accordance with the regulations on the reduction and exemption of land taxes promulgated by the Executive Yuan. The county government yesterday posted a notice with the original regulations attached, limiting the people to report to the county for verification within 20 days. The notice is recorded as follows: It is noted that the regulations on the reduction and exemption of land taxes have been formulated, promulgated, and implemented by the Executive Yuan, and the Land Administration Bureau has followed the provincial order to copy and issue the original regulations and send them to the district offices for reference. Now that this county has changed to collecting land value tax this year, all land with reduced and exempted taxes should be re-verified in accordance with the aforementioned regulations. It is appropriate to post the regulations on the reduction and exemption of land taxes for public knowledge. All institutions, organizations, or people's land that meet the standards for reduced and exempted taxes in Chapter 2 of the regulations should, within 20 days from the date of this notice, have the person in charge of the institution, the representative of the organization, or the owner himself, report the Qingzhang land number and the reason for the reduction and exemption of taxes in detail to this government for verification.

Dredging Zhangjiatang River, Estimated to Be More Than Ten Miles Long, Can Be Completed in Two Months 119

Zhangjiatang River in the Caoxing District of Western Shanghai, which connects to the Huangpu River in the east and reaches Taihu Lake via Meilong, Xinzhuang, and Sijing in the west, is an important channel for inland river traffic. Unfortunately, it has been in disrepair for many years and is increasingly silted up. Now, Yang Xinzheng, a member of the municipal government in the district, etc., has petitioned the municipal government to allocate funds for dredging. After the Port Authority sent personnel to investigate, they decided to start from the railway bridge at Xipailou and end at Xinzhuang Town to the west, which is more than ten miles long. The measurement has been completed, and water will be drained immediately to start construction. It is expected that it will be completed in February.

Dredging Bureau Tugboat Sinks Fishing Boat 124

The Zhejiang Wenzhou fishing boat Zheng Shuntai Ou Zi No. 328 loaded firewood chips and stone chips from Ou to Shanghai. After unloading, it loaded umbrellas, bamboo stones, alkali, and other southern goods to Zhejiang. It exited Shanghai at 2 pm on the previous day (the 26th) and sailed to the ferry pier in Gaoqiao City. Suddenly, a tugboat of the Dredging Bureau towed an iron-shelled mud barge and exited from the rear. Because the tugboat was going too fast, it collided with the port side of the Zheng Shuntai, and water entered the cabin and sank immediately. After the accident, the tugboat did not stop and continued to sail away. Seven crew members of the fishing boat, Xie Guixian, etc., swam to the shore and landed, so they were not drowned. The shipowner, Zheng Huanshan, suffered heavy losses because the ship and goods were all sunk. Moreover, the area is an important channel for ships to enter and exit, and he is afraid of obstructing navigation. He specially asked Yang Bao and the customs broker to file a report with the Zhanghuabang Customs Hebos Division, requesting that measures be taken to salvage the sunken ship and negotiate with the Dredging Bureau for valuation and compensation in order to uphold justice and maintain shipping.

French Concession Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter Requesting Legal Searches, Respecting Residents' Freedom, and Not Allowing Arbitrary Infringement 125

The Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association recently investigated and found that there are more than 500,000 residents in this concession. Now that it is severe winter, petty thieves are active, and robberies, etc., are frequently heard. They have already sent a letter to the police authorities asking them to pay attention. Moreover, the association believes that residents who are suspected of committing crimes must be searched when necessary. However, in the spirit of a country ruled by law, the residence and body of the people should be absolutely free and inviolable except in accordance with legal procedures. In the past, there were always those who broke into people's homes without holding a court search warrant, which was really inappropriate. The association has sent a letter to the French Municipal Council, asking the French authorities that in the future, if there is a situation of searching residents, they should follow legal procedures and not infringe on the freedom of the people, etc. After receiving the letter, the French Municipal Council has separately replied to the association, saying that the requested letter has been forwarded to the French Consul-General for review.

Reasons for the Decline of Chinese Tea in the Dutch East Indies: Japanese Tea and Local Tea Rise to Compete, 12,000 Unemployed Chinese Merchants 126

China's tea exports have always been sold to Europe, America, and various parts of Southeast Asia. Recently, due to the willful squeeze of tea grown in Europe and America and tea from India and Ceylon, Chinese tea has plummeted. Sales in Southeast Asia are also in a very dangerous situation. A reporter from Shenzhou News Agency learned from various parties such as tea exporters and overseas Chinese affairs agencies in this port that tea sales in Southeast Asia have been maintained in the past three years. Recently, due to the dumping of Japanese tea and the gradual development of local tea businesses by natives, the Chinese tea market is far from as good as before. The Dutch East Indies tea market has always been uniquely popular with Chinese tea, with annual sales of about several million yuan. There are more than 20,000 Chinese engaged in this industry, and three times as many people depend on it for a living, directly or indirectly. They are quite profitable and occupy an important position in the economy of overseas Chinese. However, six or seven years ago, the Dutch East Indies government was determined to promote local tea planting and sent specialized personnel to guide it. It has had significant results and encouraged residents to buy and drink local tea. Moreover, local tea is cheap, and to this day, local natives and local-born Chinese are happy to use it. Chinese tea has therefore been greatly impacted. In addition, Japanese and Taiwanese tea are also being sold in an attempt to implement their Nanhua policy. Chinese tea is therefore more suppressed. This year, the input of Chinese tea to the Dutch East Indies has greatly declined compared to last year. Last spring, the input of Chinese tea to the Dutch East Indies was 3,000 kilograms, and Japanese and Taiwanese tea, according to the report of the Dutch East Indies Chamber of Commerce, reached more than 1.4 million kilograms. This year, it will be even more active. At present, Chinese tea is in a slump and is in danger of complete collapse. Currently, 70% of Chinese stores that purely operate Chinese tea have closed down. The number of overseas Chinese who have lost their jobs as a result has reached 12,000 to date. More than 9,000 people have returned to their ancestral home due to unemployment. The impact on the lives of overseas Chinese is very serious. The main reason for the collapse of the Chinese tea market is that the cost is too high to compete. Overseas Chinese are paying close attention to this.

Pei Jinfu Accused of Seducing Female Servant 127

Zhao Shen, a 53-year-old woman from Gaoyou, Jiangbei, who lives at No. 58 Boxiang Village, Laozhenfu Road, French Concession, recently hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Special Second Court, accusing Pei Jinfu, a fellow villager residing at No. 15 Jianye Lane, Fulvli Road, of seducing and hiding her daughter, requesting investigation, and attaching a civil suit to recover her daughter. According to the complaint, the plaintiff's daughter, nicknamed Abao, is 20 years old this year. In August of last year, she came to Shanghai with neighbors to work as a servant. It was not known that after arriving in Shanghai, there was no news. It was not until the beginning of October in the old calendar this year that the plaintiff came to Shanghai to look for her and learned that she was working as a servant in the defendant's house. After being seduced into adultery, she was not allowed to communicate with her family. She has already given birth to a son after being raped. The defendant has violated Article 240, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, the crime of obstructing morality. Moreover, the plaintiff's daughter has been betrothed to a man in her hometown and is scheduled to be married in the first month of next year. The defendant already has two wives and concubines. When the plaintiff went to find her daughter, the defendant prevented her from meeting. She requests that the defendant be investigated and handled according to law. According to the complaint, the court summoned the plaintiff, Zhao Shen, and her lawyer to the court for questioning on the morning of the day before. The defendant was not present. The court ordered that the defendant be summoned again on the 30th for questioning.

After Shortening the Expiration Date, the Pawnshop Business Gradually Turns Around 128

This year, the first batch of pawnshops in this city will expire on New Year's Day. Due to the influence of falling prices and changes in the style of full goods for many years, most of them have suffered losses. Therefore, in December of last year, they submitted an application to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to change the expiration date of pawned goods to twelve months (originally eighteen months) in order to save the crisis. From New Year's Day this year, all pawnshops in the city have been implementing this uniformly. In this way, the storage time is reduced, and the sale of goods is not as easy to suffer losses as in the past. At the same time, this year, the price of goods has risen, and the selling price of full goods has also increased accordingly. Therefore, pawnshops this year have shown vitality. Moreover, since the industry implemented the shortening of the pawn period from New Year's Day this year, it will be twelve months until New Year's Day next year. Therefore, a notice will be published in the newspaper in the coming days to urge pawnshop customers to redeem their goods.

Tobacco Exchange Industry Association Notice, Change to Spring License as Scheduled 132

The South Shanghai Office of the Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Industry Association yesterday notified its members: Notice is hereby given that the time for changing tobacco and alcohol license taxes is approaching the end of winter and the beginning of spring. According to the regulations, the period for exchanging new licenses is from January 1st to the 10th. Those who exceed the time limit will be punished. All members of our association must, within the time limit, send the spring tax due, together with the old license and business status, for filling in and exchanging new licenses. If there is anything unclear in the procedures, you can send it to this office (No. 427 Fumin Road, Danankou) before January 10th for registration and reporting, so that we can exchange the new license on your behalf. Do not neglect it, so as not to violate the punishment. This notice is hereby given.

Amendment to the Regulations for Managing Prepared Medicines; Notice from the New Medicine Association; Effective January 1st 133

The National Federation of New Medicine Associations yesterday issued a notice to its members nationwide, stating that the Ministry of Health of the Executive Yuan had approved document number Yi Zi 7358, regarding the review of the Regulations for Managing Prepared Medicines. These regulations were promulgated and implemented by the former Ministry of Health in the 19th year of the Republic [1930] and have been in effect for six years. Several provisions are no longer suited to the actual situation, and the permissible limits of narcotic drugs in prepared medicines require revision. Previously, numerous Chinese and foreign pharmaceutical merchants had requested amendments, and opinions were solicited from various parties for consideration. Simultaneously, a general registration of prepared medicines was conducted to meet current needs. Subsequently, the revised Regulations for Managing Prepared Medicines were completed and a draft was submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. Now, Directive No. 4274, issued on November 28th of the 25th year of the Republic [1936], has been received, approving the record for future reference. Article 15 of the revised regulations stipulates that the effective date of these regulations shall be determined by the Ministry of Health through an order. Furthermore, the general registration of prepared medicines had previously been extended to cease on November 30th of this year. These revised regulations are now scheduled to take effect on January 1st of the 26th year of the Republic [1937]. In addition to separate announcements and communications, and reporting the effective date to the Executive Yuan for record, copies of the revised regulations are hereby issued for the association's information and for dissemination to all colleagues in the industry. This notice is for your attention. Accordingly, a copy of the aforementioned revised regulations is enclosed, and it is hoped that you will take note and disseminate this information.

Revised Regulations for Managing Prepared Medicines:

Article 1: Any medicinal material that has been processed and prepared, not using its original name, with the intention of being used for the treatment of diseases without a doctor's prescription, clearly indicating its efficacy, dosage, and usage, and sold directly, shall be considered a prepared medicine.

Article 2: Anyone preparing or importing prepared medicines shall fill out a prepared medicine examination request form, along with samples and leaflets, and submit them to the Ministry of Health for examination and approval. Only after obtaining a prepared medicine permit shall they be allowed to sell it. The format of the aforementioned prepared medicine examination request form will be determined separately.

Article 3: When submitting a request for examination and a permit, a certificate fee of two yuan shall be prepaid for each type of prepared medicine, and trial fees and stamp duties shall be paid in accordance with regulations. If the prepared medicine submitted for examination is not approved by the Ministry of Health, the aforementioned prepaid fees shall be refunded. However, the trial fee will not be refunded if the medicine has already been chemically tested.

Article 4: When manufacturers or importers of prepared medicines obtain a permit and commence business, they shall immediately submit the permit or a copy of the permit issued by the Ministry of Health to the provincial or municipal (municipality directly under the Executive Yuan) health authorities in the place of business. The provincial or municipal (municipality directly under the Executive Yuan) health authorities shall review the aforementioned submitted documents, and if there are no errors, they shall promptly issue an approval for business operations and shall not charge any fees.

Article 5: Only pharmaceutical merchants are allowed to prepare or import prepared medicines. Western pharmaceutical merchants preparing prepared medicines must employ a pharmacist.

Article 6: The amount of morphine added to prepared medicines shall not exceed two parts per thousand, and the amount of coca root shall not exceed one part per thousand. The amount of other narcotic drugs added shall be determined by the Ministry of Health, but heroin shall not be added. Those who prepare or import prepared medicines containing narcotic drugs shall keep separate registers, recording the quantity and the name and address of the place of sale on a daily basis for inspection.

Article 7: If prepared medicines contain toxic drugs listed in the Chinese Pharmacopoeia, the dosage shall not exceed one-third of the dosage listed. If they are not listed in the Chinese Pharmacopoeia, the dosage shall be determined by the Ministry of Health.

Article 8: For all approved prepared medicines, the dosage, the names of the main medicinal materials contained, the business name, and the permit number must be clearly stated on the container label or packaging insert before they can be displayed and sold. The aforementioned main medicinal materials shall be specified by the Ministry of Health when approving the permit.

Article 9: The advertisements, inserts, and information attached to the containers or packaging of prepared medicines shall not contain any of the following: (1) Words or pictures involving obscenity or aphrodisiac seeds; (2) Sentences implying abortion, etc.; (3) False, exaggerated, superstitious, or guarantees of efficacy in the name of others, which are liable to cause misunderstanding; (4) Statements implying the ineffectiveness of medical treatment or containing words of ridicule against doctors; (5) Inappropriate instructions on dosage.

Article 10: The competent health authorities in the place of business may dispatch pharmaceutical professionals to conduct on-site investigations of the places where prepared medicines are prepared, imported, or sold at any time. The Ministry of Health may directly dispatch personnel for inspection when necessary.

Article 11: If those who prepare or import prepared medicines violate these regulations or the orders or decisions issued in accordance with these regulations, unless there are penalties specified in other articles, the penalties in those articles shall apply. The competent health authorities in the place of business may report the violation to the Ministry of Health and request the revocation of the permit.

Article 12: Those who sell prepared medicines without obtaining a prepared medicine permit in accordance with Article 2, or violate the provisions of Article 6 or Article 7, may be fined up to thirty yuan by the competent health authorities in the place of business with the approval of the Ministry of Health, and the prepared medicines that violate the regulations shall be prohibited from sale or confiscated.

Article 13: Those who violate the provisions of Article 5, Article 8, or Article 9, and those who refuse the inspection in Article 10 shall be fined up to twenty yuan.

Article 14: Matters concerning the business of prepared medicines shall be governed by the Regulations for Managing Pharmaceutical Merchants, unless otherwise provided in these regulations.

Article 15: The effective date of these regulations shall be determined by the Ministry of Health through an order.

Hardware Store Apprentice Sentenced for Fraud; Sentenced to One Year and Seven Months, Suspended for Three Years; Receiver of Stolen Goods Fined 100 Yuan 141

Jin Youding, a 17-year-old apprentice from Ningbo at Hengxin Hardware Store, 67 Yongji Lane, Tangshan Road, was found to have privately issued invoices and stamped them with the Hengxin seal between March and November of this year, defrauding the following hardware stores on Broadway of steel plates, lead sheets, and iron bars worth 834.15 yuan: Yuantai, Tongyihe, Chengfu, and others. The court ordered the apprentice Jin to be detained, and Hua paid a 1,000 yuan security deposit. Yesterday, Judge Zhong Qing presided over Criminal Court No. 3, and after a thorough investigation, Jin Youding was sentenced to one year and seven months of imprisonment, suspended for three years, and Hua Ronggen was fined 100 yuan. If the fine is not paid, Hua will be required to perform labor for the equivalent of two yuan per day. The civil suit was transferred to the Civil Court for handling.

Postal Knowledge Questions (4) 145

Question: "In your last Q&A, you stated that ordinary stamps either have an image of Dr. Sun Yat-sen or various martyrs. It seems that there are no other designs. However, I recently purchased several kinds of stamps with sailing ship designs from the post office. What is the reason for this?"

Answer: The stamps with the images of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and the martyrs are the new version of stamps that have been successively issued since 1931. The stamps with sailing ship and train designs are older stamps that are still available in post offices, so they are being sold at the same time as the new version. The types of these old version stamps are as follows:

1. Ordinary stamps with sailing ship and train designs: There are eleven denominations: ½ fen, 1 fen, 1½ fen, 2 fen, 3 fen, 4 fen, 5 fen, 6 fen, 7 fen, 8 fen, 1 jiao.

Stamps with agricultural harvest designs: There are six denominations: 1 jiao 3 fen, 1 jiao 5 fen, 1 jiao 6 fen, 2 jiao, 3 jiao, 5 jiao.

Stamps with a round gate design: There are five denominations: 1 yuan, 2 yuan, 5 yuan, 10 yuan, 20 yuan.

2. Airmail stamps: Printed in two colors, with an image of an airplane and the Great Wall, and the Kuomintang emblem on the tail. There are five denominations: 1 jiao 5 fen, 3 jiao, 4 jiao 5 fen, 6 jiao, 9 jiao.

3. Postage due stamps: Blue and brown, with the words "欠資" (Postage Due) printed in the center. There are eight denominations: ½ fen, 1 fen, 2 fen, 4 fen, 5 fen, 1 jiao, 2 jiao, 3 jiao.

The sale of all of the above stamps, along with single and double postcards with sailing ship and train designs and stationery with a Jiahe design, will be limited to December 31 of this year. Starting January 1, 1937, they will all be discontinued. Within one month after the discontinuation (i.e., from January 1 to January 31, 1937), the public can still use the above-mentioned ordinary stamps, airmail stamps, postcards, or stationery as usual. However, starting February 1, 1937, they will be completely abolished and will no longer be valid. However, if the public still has unused items at that time, they can, within six months after the abolition (i.e., from February 1 to July 31, 1937), exchange them for new versions of ordinary or airmail stamps or new versions of postcards (with Dr. Sun Yat-sen stamp) or special postal cards (with 5 fen Dr. Sun Yat-sen stamp) at the local post office according to the face value. The new version of postcards are only available in single cards of 1 fen (local delivery), 2½ fen (domestic), 1 jiao 5 fen (international), and double cards of 2 fen, 5 fen, 3 jiao, and 6 jiao. For example, if someone has an old 6 fen single postcard and exchanges it at the post office, they can receive ordinary stamps worth 6 fen, or two 2½ fen postcards and one 1 fen postcard, or six 1 fen postcards. In short, the value of the items exchanged must be equal to the original face value. The same applies to the public who has old versions of postage due stamps and wants to exchange them for new versions of stamps, postcards, or special postal cards.

Local Security Guard Xu Tingzhong Shot Dead by Zhang Jinbao; Police Strictly Investigating Zhang 149

On the evening of the second day of last month, at around 8:00 pm, in the Xujiaqiao area of Zhabei, a local security guard named Xu Tingzhong was ambushed by multiple thugs armed with pistols and was fatally wounded on the spot. Details of the incident have been reported in this newspaper. It has now been learned that the police have determined that the mastermind behind the murder was the notorious gangster Zhang Jinbao (nicknamed "Bandit Jinbao"). Zhang was previously arrested by the Public Concession Police for theft and possession of illegal firearms, and was interrogated and sentenced by the First Special District Court to imprisonment, which he served at Tilanqiao Prison. While Zhang was in prison, his concubine, Ms. Lin, worked at the Zhongxing Silk Factory on Tianbao Road and had an affair with a factory employee named Yu. Zhang learned of the affair after his release and, in a fit of jealousy, secretly plotted revenge. However, his plans were discovered by Ms. Lin and Yu, who, fearing for their lives, informed the Songhu Garrison Headquarters through Yu about Zhang's possession of red pills and other drugs. The Garrison Headquarters ordered an investigation team to search Zhang's house in conjunction with the police. A large number of red pills were found on the spot, but Zhang was out and was not arrested. With the evidence confirmed, the Garrison Headquarters issued a warrant for his arrest and sealed his house. Zhang, suspecting that the local security guard Xu Tingzhong had instigated the affair, retaliated against Xu by instructing his accomplices to shoot him. After the incident, Zhang fled to the Wusong countryside. The police dispatched officers to arrest him, but Zhang fled without a trace. A strict investigation is underway to arrest and punish him.

(3) Liu Changxian, a lawyer from Nanjing, representing the Zhengtaixiang and other glass companies in Nanjing, published a notice claiming that the association was increasing donations. It was resolved that lawyer Zhu Yakui, the association's legal counsel, publish a reply based on the facts, stating that the association was collecting stacking fees in accordance with the regulations that had been approved and recorded, and that it was not increasing donations, but was deliberately slandering the association. (4) It was resolved to notify all members to participate in the rally to celebrate Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing, which would be held at the Public Sports Ground at 2 p.m. on the 28th, and Yao Qiusheng and Jin Fumo were appointed as marshals (remaining items omitted).

Shanghai's Electrical Manufacturing Industry (Continued) 166

— Chief Editor, China Credit Information

(A General Survey of Shanghai Industry and Commerce, Part 40)

As for the market conditions for electrical materials this year, they were initially flat, but after entering autumn, they began to flourish. During this period, due to the unstable situation, customers stocked up on goods, and sales were even stronger. Batteries, flashlights, and electrical materials with military applications were naturally in demand, but even ordinary light bulbs suddenly became in short supply. According to a report in the Dagongbao on November 3rd, the major factories in this city that produce these goods were all busy, and in September some even opened night shifts to increase production to meet market demand. Although some businesses in the industry have recently failed, this is mainly due to long-term mismanagement, not a sudden occurrence. The production and sales of the major factories are briefly described below: In the fall, the A. O. Ear factory had the highest light bulb production and total sales, producing 2.5 million bulbs with a transaction value of about 500,000 yuan. Next was the Huade factory, which produced 440,000 to 450,000 bulbs with a sales value of 200,000 yuan. The Fulai Sheng factory was next, with a production volume exceeding the Huade factory at 500,000 bulbs, but because they were all low-priced bulbs, the sales volume was lower than that of the Huade factory, at only 40,000 yuan. The Yongming factory was next, producing 400,000 bulbs, with a sales value of 54,000 to 55,000 yuan, including the sale of electric beads. Currently, although the sales of light bulbs in the Shanghai market are more active than last season, the market price situation has not increased due to the stable price of raw materials. However, small factories have had to secretly lower their prices to distribute their goods due to the impact of the extremely low-priced, unbranded light bulbs sold on the market. However, the products of major factories can be sold according to their original prices. As for colored light bulbs, such as three-way bulbs and five-way multi-filament bulbs, their unique manufacturing means that they are not as affected by the large number of products as ordinary light bulbs, and they are also not affected by the dumping of unbranded foreign goods. Therefore, the market price is slightly better than other ordinary products. For example, the Central Factory's three-way bulb sells for 40 cents in national currency, but in order to promote sales, it is also necessary to reduce the price slightly.

The market prices of various electrical materials have recently shown a significant upward trend due to the influence of the domestic and foreign situation. Insulated wire and flower wire have already increased by 20% compared to before. Other products are related to foreign raw materials, and manufacturers must increase prices in order to protect their capital. However, sales are even more difficult after the price increase, which is a major difficulty for operators. (End)
