Movies

The Actors of "Soaring Ambitions" 191

Speaking of Jin Yan, it can be said that there is no one who does not know him. Indeed, Jin Yan's impression on the screen is very deep. It is not an exaggeration to say that he earned the highest praise of "Movie Emperor" among all Chinese male actors, and it is definitely not accidental, which shows that he has true talent. Now, in "Soaring Ambitions," playing Shun'er, his vigorous performance and powerful actions profoundly express the heroic nature of a resolute and decisive youth, with astonishing success.

Wang Renmei Just like Jin Yan, Ms. Wang Renmei is also a movie actor that you cannot forget. In the past, Ms. Wang has always been loved by the audience for her innocent and wild performances. Since her marriage, it was generally thought that she would change her style, but actually not at all. In this "Soaring Ambitions," she plays a strong and spicy wild girl. Perhaps because she has more rich experience in life, she performs the role of Black Girl even more skillfully.

Wang Cilong It would not be wrong to crown Wang Cilong with the title of "Veteran General" of the silver screen. Wang Cilong is truly a versatile person in the film industry. For more than ten years, he has always been working hard for his future, and never slackens because of the rise of talented younger generations. In "Soaring Ambitions," he plays a traitor, and through his calm and experienced acting skills, he vividly portrays the treacherous and cunning demeanor of the traitor, making people really feel that he is a bad guy.

Han Langen The only clown on the current film scene. The fact that his comedic actions contain the serious meaning of life is the unique aspect of Mr. Han's acting skills. In "Soaring Ambitions," he plays a cowardly youth who is generally considered to be unsuccessful, but in the end, he makes a great sacrifice to protect the national flag. The profoundness of his acting is truly thought-provoking.

Tian Fang It has been a long time since we parted ways with Tian Fang after "Good Land". That's right, Mr. Tian's ambition is worthy of our praise. He knows that his acting skills are not yet outstanding, so he has been silent, but striving for the cultivation of his art. Now, in "Soaring Ambitions," he makes a comeback, and he has indeed given us great satisfaction. He plays Tian Dehou, a youth who transforms from selfish and self-interested to heroic sacrifice, and expresses several layers of personality, without any laxity that we can criticize.

Four Major Stars Co-Star in "The Wife Stealer" 192

As the New Year approaches, amidst this atmosphere of universal joy, the Nanjing Grand Theater's contribution to the honor of Shanghai residents is the public screening, starting January 1st of next year, of MGM's exceptionally humorous blockbuster, "The Wife Stealer." This film is a great comedy co-starring four radiant stars from Hollywood. The cast includes the passionately romantic Jean Harlow, star of "Suzy," the witty and humorous William Powell, star of "Miss China," the expressive Myrna Loy, star of "The Great Ziegfeld," and the ruggedly straightforward Spencer Tracy, star of "Fury." With four major stars co-starring in one film, its value is evident. The story is extremely fresh and touching, centering around a man "borrowing" a wife as the core of the entire film. From this starting point, countless branches and layers of humor arise. During the New Year's holiday season, this film is truly a must-see for Shanghai movie fans.

A Word on "Street Angel" 193

Yuan Muzhi, the director and screenwriter of "Street Angel," says: The theme and style of this story are completely different from his "Cityscape." In "Street Angel," there isn't a single character wearing beautiful clothes; the story is entirely a sketch of the lives of people at the very bottom of society.

"Street Angel" features singers, news vendors, barbers, musicians, children buying pears, prostitutes, procuresses, etc.

"The Adventures of Robin Hood" Star Errol Flynn 194

Heroic Posture in the New Film "The Adventures of Robin Hood"

"Street Angel" contains two songs, imitations of folk songs, "Crying for the Seventh of July" and "Intimate [Missing Text] Read and Get [Missing Text]". Tian Han wrote the lyrics.

Zhao Huishen plays a prostitute who has been forgotten, having lived a life of flesh for many years. She is a portrayal of the many women wandering the streets, despised by people. Wei Heling has great sympathy for her.

Street angels live nocturnal lives. Since filming began, director Yuan Muzhi has been working until dawn every night.

"Street Angel" recently borrowed the Xiaoyao Bathhouse to film a bathing scene, offering many gimmicks.

China United Broadcasting 195

"China United Symphony" is a masterpiece of collaboration by all directors and stars of China United. It has now been completed and will premiere in Shanghai on New Year's Day in the 26th year [of the Republic, likely 1937]. The entire film is divided into eight parts, directed by eight people. Their order is: Situ Huimin's "Two Pennies," Fei Mu's "Spring Boudoir Broken Dream," Tan Youliu's "Stormy Night," Shen Fu's "Trio," He Mengfu's "Moonlit Sketch," Zhu Shilin's "Grandson's Ghost", Sun Yu's "Lunatic's Rhapsody" and Cai Chusheng's "Little Five Heroes."

"Little Five Heroes" is one of the liveliest and longest segments of "China United Symphony," with more than two hundred child actors joining in cameo roles. It is anticipated [Missing Text], co-starring child stars Wen Nannan, Cao Weidong, Ge Zuozhi, Tang Zhenbao and Miao Zhenyu, all lively, innocent, clever and lovely.

Fei Mu's "Spring Boudoir Broken Dream" uses sound and music entirely to represent dialogue. Although the actors in the entire segment do not speak, it never feels like anything is missing. Its transcendent design and novel concept are unprecedented.

He Mengfu's segment "Moonlit Sketch" is entirely composed by musician Sha Mei, with six-part chorus. It is performed and voiced by Lang Yuxiu, completely filled with Chinese flavor, with the sentimental air of a poet, like a short essay from the Qi Liang period.

"A Match Made in Heaven" features a scene of the Zhong Qin Factory, operated by Liu Jiqun, which is large in scale, accommodating two thousand workers, bustling and lively. Han [Missing Text] Langan once owned a bank and invented a chicken farming method. Using scientific methods to raise chickens, the eggs laid were ten inches in diameter and weighed ten pounds, the largest eggs in the world.

In Sun Yu's new work "Spring Returns to the World," the trench scene used Studio One and Studio Two connected in haste. Because of its ingenious design, it looked desolate. In order to achieve realism, the City Security Team was specially asked to lend four machine guns and more than five hundred rifles, firing live ammunition, the sound of gunfire thundering, and bullets like rain. Cameraman Huang Shaofen almost didn't dare to step forward to film.
